```txt
      09-build-equation.md
      10-solved-machinery-gates-decide.md
      11-santo-andre-lab-modus-operandi.md
```

Observação: App Park apareceu duplicado. Deve virar **um único doc canônico**.

## B. Vai como founding / operating packet v0

Estes entram também, mas não como “parent canon universal”. Eles são **Minilab operating foundation**:

```txt
01 - Minilab Founding Act
02 - Organs and Jurisdictions
03 - Source of Truth Map
04 - LLM Offices
05 - Morning State Ritual
```

```txt
docs.logline.foundation/
  minilab/
    operating-foundation/
      01-founding-act.md
      02-organs-and-jurisdictions.md
      03-source-of-truth-map.md
      04-llm-offices.md
      05-morning-state-ritual.md
      06-current-state-v0.md
      07-ghost-registry-v0.md
```

Nota: `06-current-state-v0` é mais “estado bootstrap” do que canon permanente. Entra na biblioteca como **seed/state document**, não como lei eterna. O próprio Current State diz que estado atual não é canon, receipt ou prova; é visão operacional corrente. `06_current_state_v_0.md`

## C. Vai como operations / process runtime

Estes entram, mas precisam virar versão final:

```txt
Minilab - Catálogo de Processos Operacionais v0.1
09 - Vertical Runtime Doctrine  // criado agora no canvas
10 - Hermes Dispatch and Execution Contract  // falta escrever
```

Destino sugerido:

```txt
docs.logline.foundation/
  minilab/
    operations/
      08-process-catalog.md
      09-vertical-runtime-doctrine.md
      10-hermes-dispatch-execution-contract.md
```

Aqui a regra é: o **Catálogo de Processos** entra, mas precisa receber o bloco `runtime_dynamics` em cada processo. Sem isso, ele é um bom runbook; com isso, vira processo constitucional. O doc vertical que acabamos de criar serve exatamente para essa ponte.

## D. Vai como implementation / mini-LLM substrate

Estes entram como specs de implementação, não como doutrina constitucional:

```txt
MINI-LLMS-RS-SPEC-v0.5
MINI-LLMS-RS-MATH-CONTRACT-v0.1
PR-001-LAB512-LOGLINE-DB-RUNBOOK-v0.1
```

Destino sugerido:

```txt
docs.logline.foundation/
  minilab/
    implementation/
      mini-llms/
        mini-llms-rs-spec-v0.5.md
        mini-llms-rs-math-contract-v0.1.md
        pr-001-lab512-logline-db-runbook-v0.1.md
```

O spec tem posição correta: `mini-llms.rs proposes; Constitutional Runtime admits; Tower authorizes power; LABs execute; Supabase projects; Receipts close; Dan signs consequence.` `MINI-LLMS-RS-SPEC-v0.5.md`

## E. Vai como guide, mas sanitizado

```txt
chatgpt_control_plane_implementation(5).md
```

Esse vai para biblioteca, mas **não cru**. Ele deve virar um guia sanitizado:

```txt
docs.logline.foundation/
  minilab/
    control-plane/
      chatgpt-control-plane-v0.md
```

Motivo: ele define a implementação v0 usando ChatGPT Business UI, sem API, backend, CLI, bridge ou worker; Projects são jurisdições, chats são act threads, instructions são soft-code, files são mounted context e Dan é executor manual de configuração. `chatgpt_control_plane_implementation.md`

Mas removeria detalhes privados ou excessivamente operacionais antes de publicar.

---

# 3. O que ajudou no pensamento, mas NÃO vai cru para a biblioteca

Estes não devem entrar como docs oficiais brutos.

## Não entra cru: `Forma Final Total`

```txt
Forma Final Total - Minilab como Control Plane LogLine montado sobre infraestrutura existente(2).md
```

Destino correto:

```txt
archive/thinking/
```

ou

```txt
source-notes/
```

Ele é síntese excelente, mas tem tom de conversa e “alma clause”. Deve ser **absorvido** por:

```txt
01-minilab-constitution.md
09-vertical-runtime-doctrine.md
10-hermes-dispatch-execution-contract.md
overview/minilab-assembled-system.md
```

Não entra cru. Entra como matéria-prima.

## Não entra como doctrine: `code-as-exhaust`

```txt
code-as-exhaust(5).md
```

Destino correto:

```txt
essays/
```

ou

```txt
archive/thinking/
```

Ele é ensaio conceitual. Pode virar artigo público, manifesto ou nota editorial. Mas não é documento operacional de Minilab. A tese dele informa a biblioteca, mas não deve governar a biblioteca.

## Não entra cru: `Plano Estratégico - PDF`

```txt
Plano Estratégico - Arquitetura Minilab Max Automation.pdf
```

Destino correto:

```txt
archive/legacy-strategy/
```

Ele ajudou a fundar a separação CLI/Rust, Cloudflare como edge, LABs como ambientes de execução e “database is machinery; receipt is proof”. Mas já foi supersedido por Constituição, Ontology, Database Canon e App Park docs. `Plano Estratégico — Arquitetura Minilab Max Automation.pdf`

## Não entra cru: documento dos 9 slots com título longo

```txt
who, did, this, when, confirmed_by, if_ok, if_doubt, if_not, status (1) 2(1).md
```

Destino correto:

```txt
foundation/reference/
```

mas renomeado e extraído:

```txt
logline-receipt-v0-hashing-and-conformance-notes.md
```

Ele tem material normativo valioso sobre `tuple_hash`, `content_hash`, `envelope_hash`, JCS, valid/invalid vectors e LIP-0007. Mas o arquivo cru é uma mistura de deep-dive, path local, notas e análise. Deve virar referência limpa, não entrar com esse nome. `who, did, this, when, confirmed_by, if_ok, if_doubt, if_not, status (1) 2.md`

## Não entra cru: `Lab Operator Dispatch package`

```txt
Lab Operator Dispatch package(1).md
```

Destino correto:

```txt
archive/operator-packets/
```

ou extração para:

```txt
10-hermes-dispatch-execution-contract.md
```

O pacote específico não é canon. O que entra na biblioteca é a **taxonomia e o contrato**: inspection, mutation, code, verification, intelligence, research, publication, communication; authority level; expected evidence; rollback; human check; receipt path.

## Não entram duplicados

```txt
08_app_park_primordial_packet_v_0_1 (1)(2).md
08_app_park_primordial_packet_v_0_1 (1)(3).md

04_llm_offices (1)(1).md
04_llm_offices(1).md
```

Escolhe um canonical, deduplica, preserva o outro em archive se houver diferença relevante.

# 5. O que ainda falta

Falta **um doc principal**:

```txt
10 - Hermes Dispatch and Execution Contract
```

Ele deve transformar:

```txt
Process Catalog
+ Vertical Runtime Doctrine
+ Dispatch Package taxonomy
+ Hermes/LAB execution boundary
```

em contrato final:

```txt
Process
→ Dispatch Packet
→ Authority Classification
→ Hermes Workorder
→ Execution Report
→ Evidence Record
→ Receipt Candidate / Ghost
→ Current State Projection
```

E faltam docs operacionais menores já apontados pelos ghosts:

```txt
PROMOTION_RECORD v0
LAB_INVENTORY v0
HOME_OPS_PLAN v0
SANTO_ANDRE_EXPERIMENT_REGISTRY v0
DAN_MANUAL_ACTIONS v0
EVIDENCE_REGISTRY v0
RECEIPT_REGISTRY v0
WORK_REQUEST_LEDGER v0
```

Mas esses são **state/ledger docs**, não mais teoria.

A biblioteca final não é “todos os arquivos enviados”. A biblioteca final é a versão limpa desta cadeia:

```txt
Constitution
→ Organs
→ Sources
→ Offices
→ Rites
→ State
→ Ghosts
→ Processes
→ Vertical Runtime
→ Hermes Dispatch
→ Evidence/Receipts
→ Projection
```

Essa é a linha boa.

## Prompt:
5/26/2026, 4:22:57 PM

e vamos de 

10 — Hermes Dispatch and Execution Contract

## Response:
5/26/2026, 4:23:02 PM

> **Criando o documento final sem citações diretas**
>
> Parece que o objetivo é criar um novo documento, provavelmente em um canvas. O usuário pediu um total de 10 documentos, então precisamos garantir que o novo arquivo esteja robusto e faça uso dos documentos anteriores sem repetir. A criação do documento será feita no formato adequado, sem citações, mas podemos citar fontes na versão final.
>
> **Criando um documento com detalhes específicos**
>
> Igualando ao pedido de um documento básico com "Hermes", vou criar dez seções, incluindo o propósito, regras de transição, categorias de autoridade, exemplos e outras variáveis citadas. Vou garantir que não haja citações no canvas. Também vou alinhar as definições técnicas à estrutura fornecida e incluir a verificação de energia/poder conforme mencionado pelo usuário.
>
> Pensado para 1m 33s

**10 Hermes Dispatch And Execution Contract**

# 10 — Hermes Dispatch and Execution Contract

**Status:** canon candidate / execution seam draft  
**Layer:** Minilab dispatch, Hermes workorders, LAB execution, evidence return, projection boundary  
**Parents:** 01 — Minilab Founding Act; 02 — Organs and Jurisdictions; 03 — Source of Truth Map; 04 — LLM Offices; 05 — Morning State Ritual; 06 — Current State; 07 — Ghost Registry; 08 — Process Catalog; 09 — Vertical Runtime Doctrine; Authority / Power Doctrine; Evidence / Receipt Doctrine; Database Projection Canon; mini-llms.rs Spec  
**Evidence status:** doctrine-grounded, runtime-unverified  
**Runtime mutation:** none  
**World-touch:** none

---

## 0. Purpose

This document defines the seam where Minilab work leaves interpretation and may become execution.

It connects:

```txt
Process Catalog
→ Vertical Runtime Doctrine
→ Dispatch Packet
→ Authority classification
→ Hermes Workorder
→ LAB execution
→ Execution Report
→ Evidence Record
→ Receipt Candidate or Ghost
→ Current State projection
```

It exists to prevent:

```txt
free language becoming execution
operator confidence becoming dispatch
mini-LLM output becoming workorder
well-formed packet becoming authority
Hermes becoming governor
LAB identity becoming permission
stdout becoming receipt
provider success becoming closure
```

Hermes is the worker runtime.  
Hermes executes admitted work.  
Hermes does not govern.

---

## 1. Canonical Sentence

```txt
Hermes executes only admitted workorders:
dispatch packets describe work,
Constitutional Runtime admits shape,
Authority gates consequence,
Dan signs protected scope,
Hermes runs on LABs,
evidence returns,
receipts close narrowly,
and ghosts preserve what cannot honestly close.
```

Portuguese form:

```txt
Hermes executa apenas workorders admitidos:
dispatch packets descrevem trabalho,
o Constitutional Runtime admite a forma,
a Autoridade governa consequência,
Dan assina escopo protegido,
Hermes roda nos LABs,
a evidência retorna,
receipts fecham escopo,
e ghosts preservam o que não pode fechar honestamente.
```

Short form:

```txt
Dispatch describes.
Runtime admits.
Authority gates.
Hermes executes.
Evidence returns.
Receipts close.
Ghosts preserve.
```

---

## 2. Execution Law

```txt
Hermes receives workorders, not wishes.
```

No natural-language request may be sent directly to Hermes.

Correct path:

```txt
intent
→ process
→ dispatch packet
→ runtime admission
→ authority classification
→ Hermes workorder
→ LAB execution
→ evidence packet
→ receipt / ghost / projection
```

Forbidden path:

```txt
chat message
→ Hermes command
→ claimed completion
```

Hermes may execute:

```txt
read-only inspections
dry-run probes
verification commands
build/test commands
research capture jobs
local inference jobs
media processing jobs
artifact generation jobs
explicitly admitted apply operations
```

Hermes may not decide:

```txt
whether work should exist
whether a protected action is allowed
whether Dan approved consequence
whether evidence closes a claim
whether a receipt is valid
whether a ghost is resolved
```

---

## 3. Place in the Vertical Stack

```txt
Dan
  source of intent, consequence signer

Cockpit
  intake, routing, reports, decision preparation

Offices / Operators
  interpret within mandate

mini-llms.rs
  cognitive metabolism below operators

Process Catalog
  repeatable institutional trajectories

Dispatch Packet
  structured work proposal or work unit

Constitutional Runtime
  admission and semantic boundary

Authority / Gate / Window
  consequence and protected power boundary

Hermes
  worker runtime / execution hand

LABs
  physical-digital execution places

Evidence / Receipts / Ghosts
  proof, closure, and missing-proof discipline

Registry / Current State
  projection and visibility
```

Hermes sits below Authority and above LAB execution mechanics.

---

## 4. Core Objects

### 4.1 Process

A repeatable institutional trajectory from the Process Catalog.

A process defines:

```txt
trigger
organ
office
preconditions
runtime dynamics
evidence requirements
possible ghosts
next process
```

### 4.2 Dispatch Packet

A structured packet representing a proposed or prepared unit of work.

It may be read-only, advisory, code, research, publication, mutation, verification, or executable.

A dispatch packet is not execution.

### 4.3 Authority Classification

The decision about consequence surface.

Authority class may include:

```txt
read_only
advisory
proposed_mutation
code_draft
verification
research
publication_candidate
executable
protected
```

### 4.4 Hermes Workorder

An admitted executable subset of a dispatch packet.

Hermes workorders are bounded, typed, and evidence-bearing.

A workorder is not a receipt.

### 4.5 LAB

The physical or local execution environment.

LABs execute. They do not govern.

### 4.6 Execution Report

Hermes' structured return from execution.

It records what was attempted, where, when, with what status, and what evidence references exist.

### 4.7 Evidence Record

A persisted referenceable observation derived from execution, inspection, runtime contact, provider response, file hash, or manual observation.

Evidence supports closure. It is not closure.

### 4.8 Receipt Candidate

A proposed closure packet for review.

Receipt candidate is not a receipt.

### 4.9 Ghost

A structured absence blocking honest closure or execution.

---

## 5. Dispatch Packet Contract

### 5.1 Purpose

Dispatch packets make work explicit before execution.

They separate:

```txt
inspection
mutation
code manipulation
verification
intelligence
research
publication
communication
execution
```

This prevents a single attractive instruction from smuggling authority, execution, and proof closure into one step.

### 5.2 Conceptual Shape

```yaml
dispatch_version: minilab.dispatch.v0
packet_id:
correlation_id:
created_at:
created_by:

source_process:
  process_id:
  process_name:
  organ:
  office:
  jurisdiction:

packet_type:
  inspection | mutation | code | verification | intelligence | research | publication | communication | executable

authority_level:
  read_only | advisory | proposed_mutation | code_draft | verification | publish_candidate | executable | protected

objective:
input_sources: []
proposed_action:
expected_evidence: []
rollback_or_rectify:
required_human_check:
  none | Dan | reviewer | conference | external_authority

runtime_dynamics_ref:
logline_candidate_ref:
authority_packet_ref:

hermes:
  workorder_allowed: true | false
  suggested_target_lab:
  suggested_mode: read_only | dry_run | apply
  allowed_actions: []
  forbidden_actions: []

evidence_status:
  missing | planned | observed | evidence_captured | verified | ghost

receipt_path:
projection_targets: []
ghosts: []
notes:
```

### 5.3 Dispatch Packet Invariants

```txt
Every dispatch packet names its process.
Every dispatch packet names its authority level.
Every dispatch packet names expected evidence.
Every dispatch packet names rollback or rectify condition.
Every dispatch packet names required human check.
Executable dispatch must name Hermes boundary.
Protected dispatch must name Authority / Dan boundary.
Publication dispatch must name claim risk and rectification path.
```

### 5.4 Forbidden Dispatch Content

Dispatch packets must not contain:

```txt
raw secret values
unbounded shell strings without scope
implicit apply mode
hidden provider mutation
unreviewed public claim
receipt closure claim
broad verification claim
model output as evidence
Dan approval by implication
```

---

## 6. Dispatch Packet Types

### 6.1 Inspection

Read-only gathering of state or source material.

Examples:

```txt
repo tree inspection
LAB inventory inspection
recent events inventory
claim surface inspection
current state review
```

Default authority:

```txt
read_only
```

Hermes may run inspection only if admitted as read-only.

### 6.2 Mutation

Proposed change to structure, config, database, provider, repo, canon, jurisdiction, or public posture.

Default authority:

```txt
proposed_mutation
```

Requires review before execution.

### 6.3 Code

Draft code change, schema, migration, validator, generator, tool, adapter, or test.

Default authority:

```txt
code_draft
```

A code packet may produce a patch. It may not claim implementation success until verification evidence exists.

### 6.4 Verification

Commands or probes that check claims.

Default authority:

```txt
verification
```

May be executable if read-only or dry-run. Protected if it mutates, deploys, deletes, migrates, or touches external state.

### 6.5 Intelligence

Local/model-assisted analysis.

Default authority:

```txt
advisory
```

May use mini-llms.rs or local models. Output remains candidate.

### 6.6 Research

Internet or internal source research, citation capture, experiment review, or standards lookup.

Default authority:

```txt
research
```

Current factual claims require citations or evidence references.

### 6.7 Publication

Drafting or preparing public-facing material.

Default authority:

```txt
publish_candidate
```

Publication packets require claim class, risk, evidence, and rectify/delete condition.

### 6.8 Communication

Dan-facing, collaborator-facing, partner-facing, or operator-facing messages.

Default authority:

```txt
advisory
```

External or reputational messages may require Dan approval.

### 6.9 Executable

A dispatch packet intended to become a Hermes workorder.

Default authority:

```txt
executable
```

Executable dispatch must pass admission and authority classification.

---

## 7. Authority Levels

### read_only

May inspect without mutation.

Must still avoid secrets and false closure.

### advisory

May analyze, summarize, recommend, classify, or propose.

May not execute.

### proposed_mutation

May describe a mutation.

Requires review/admission before effect.

### code_draft

May draft code or schema.

Generated code is artifact, not delivery.

### verification

May run or request checks.

If checks mutate state, escalate.

### publish_candidate

May draft public material.

Publication requires claim risk review and Dan approval when needed.

### executable

May become Hermes workorder after admission.

Executable does not mean protected permission exists.

### protected

Requires Authority, Gate, Dan approval, execution window, passkey window, or receipt path as applicable.

---

## 8. Admission to Hermes Workorder

A dispatch packet may become Hermes workorder only when:

```txt
1. source process exists
2. runtime_dynamics block exists
3. packet_type allows execution
4. authority level is executable or admitted verification/code task
5. Constitutional Runtime admits shape and source
6. Authority classification does not deny
7. required Dan/reviewer approval exists if needed
8. target LAB is declared
9. power/wakefulness prerequisites are known or ghosted
10. secret policy is explicit
11. evidence requirements are explicit
12. rollback/rectify path is explicit
```

If any condition is missing, do not execute.

Open or carry a ghost.

---

## 9. Power / Electricity / Wakefulness Boundary

Hermes execution depends on physical substrate.

The minimum material prerequisites are:

```txt
machine exists
machine is powered
machine is awake or wakeable
network path exists if needed
runtime process exists or can be started under admitted scope
storage path exists
secrets/config are present by name when needed
```

Power is not authority.

Electricity makes execution possible.  
It does not make execution permitted.

If power/wakefulness is unknown:

```txt
lab-power-state-unknown
lab-sleep-prevention-unverified
host-runtime-unobserved
worker-bridge-absent
```

Hermes must not hide physical uncertainty behind a software-green status.

---

## 10. Hermes Workorder Contract

### 10.1 Purpose

A Hermes Workorder is the exact packet Hermes may execute.

It must be narrower than the dispatch packet.

A dispatch packet may contain discussion, risk, alternatives, publication context, review notes, and authority notes.

A workorder contains only admitted execution instructions.

### 10.2 Conceptual Shape

```yaml
workorder_version: hermes.workorder.v0
workorder_id:
correlation_id:
created_at:

source_dispatch_packet:
source_process:
source_logline_candidate:
authority_decision_ref:
execution_window_ref:

requested_by:
operator_office:
mode: read_only | dry_run | apply
command_class: normal | protected
risk_class: low | medium | high | critical

target:
  lab_id:
  runtime_id:
  host_ref:
  working_directory:

allowed_actions: []
forbidden_actions: []

inputs:
  refs: []
  inline: {}

commands:
  - command_id:
    kind: shell | http | sql | file | model | build | test | other
    argv: []
    env_policy:
      allow_secret_names: true
      allow_secret_values: false
    timeout_seconds:
    expected_exit_codes: []

expected_outputs: []
evidence_required:
  - kind:
    required: true | false
    redaction_required: true | false

artifact_policy:
  write_allowed: true | false
  output_root:
  retention:
  hashing_required: true

secret_policy:
  secret_values_allowed_in_logs: false
  redact_before_store: true

rollback_or_rectify:
receipt_profile:
projection_targets: []
```

### 10.3 Workorder Invariants

```txt
No workorder without source dispatch packet.
No workorder without target LAB/runtime.
No workorder without mode.
No apply workorder without authority path.
No protected workorder without required approval/window.
No workorder with secret values embedded.
No workorder without evidence requirements.
No workorder may claim receipt closure.
```

---

## 11. Execution Modes

### read_only

Reads state or files.

Forbidden:

```txt
writes
deletes
provider mutation
database semantic writes
network side effects except scoped GET/inspection
```

### dry_run

Plans or simulates effect without applying it.

Allowed:

```txt
migration plan
build plan
deploy plan
route plan
schema validation
fixture run
```

### apply

Performs effect.

Requires:

```txt
Authority admission
Dan approval when required
ExecutionWindow / PasskeyWindow when required
evidence path
rollback/rectify path
receipt profile
```

Default mode is never apply.

If mode is absent:

```txt
ghost: workorder-mode-missing
```

---

## 12. Command Discipline

Hermes commands must be bounded.

Preferred command form:

```yaml
argv:
  - cargo
  - test
  - -p
  - mini-llms
```

Avoid unbounded shell strings.

Allowed only with explicit reason:

```yaml
shell: "find docs -maxdepth 3 -type f | sort"
```

Forbidden by default:

```txt
rm -rf
curl | sh
printing env
cat .env
writing secrets to logs
unbounded recursive grep over secret areas
provider mutation without authority
silent database migration
deploy without gate
public route creation
```

---

## 13. Hermes Execution Report

### 13.1 Purpose

Execution Report is Hermes' return path.

It says what happened during execution.  
It does not close proof by itself.

### 13.2 Conceptual Shape

```yaml
report_version: hermes.execution_report.v0
report_id:
workorder_id:
correlation_id:

target_lab:
runtime_id:
started_at:
finished_at:
duration_ms:

status: observed | succeeded | failed | inconclusive | ghost | rejected
mode:

commands_run:
  - command_id:
    argv_redacted: []
    started_at:
    finished_at:
    exit_code:
    stdout_ref:
    stderr_ref:
    output_summary:
    secret_redacted: true

artifacts:
  - artifact_ref:
    kind:
    path_or_uri:
    hash:
    size_bytes:
    redaction_status:

observations:
  - kind:
    summary:
    evidence_ref:

ghosts:
  - ghost_key:
    why:
    next_probe:

runtime_claims:
  dispatcher_invoked:
  database_written:
  provider_called:
  receipt_emitted: false

next_act:
```

### 13.3 Report Status Meanings

#### observed

Execution contacted reality and produced observation, but success/closure is not asserted.

#### succeeded

The command satisfied its expected local condition.

This still does not mean broad system success.

#### failed

The command failed within declared scope.

#### inconclusive

Execution happened but did not decide the claim.

#### ghost

Execution could not honestly proceed or conclude because required runtime, source, config, authority, or evidence was missing.

#### rejected

Workorder was rejected before execution.

---

## 14. Evidence Return

Hermes reports must be transformed into Evidence Records when they matter.

Evidence records may include:

```txt
command_output
http_response
sql_result
file_hash
container_state
runtime_health
model_response
work_item_attempt
screenshot
manual_observation
```

Evidence record requirements:

```txt
scope
runtime
observed_at
producer
redaction flag
payload/artifact refs
hashes when available
secret_redacted=true
```

Evidence does not become receipt automatically.

---

## 15. Receipt Candidate Path

Receipt candidate may be prepared only after evidence exists.

Receipt candidate must state:

```txt
claim
scope
evidence refs
what this may close
what this does not close
conformance state
receipt profile
ghosts
reviewer
```

Forbidden receipt candidate claims:

```txt
the system works
the app is safe
production ready
all regressions absent
all users protected
future operations guaranteed
```

Allowed narrow claims:

```txt
this command ran with this exit code on this LAB at this time
this health endpoint returned this response
this migration dry-run produced this plan
this file was generated with this hash
this model call returned ReasoningOnlyNoContent
this candidate passed schema guard
```

---

## 16. Ghost Path

If execution cannot proceed or closure cannot be honest, open or carry a ghost.

Common Hermes ghosts:

```txt
workorder-mode-missing
target-lab-missing
lab-inventory-missing
lab-power-state-unknown
lab-sleep-prevention-unverified
host-runtime-unobserved
worker-bridge-absent
authority-decision-missing
execution-window-missing
dan-approval-missing
secret-policy-missing
evidence-return-missing
artifact-hash-missing
receipt-profile-missing
conformance-unobserved
```

Ghosts must name:

```txt
what is missing
why it blocks execution or closure
owner / organ
next act
closure condition
```

---

## 17. Database / Projection Boundary

Hermes may write operational execution records only through admitted paths.

Projection targets may include:

```txt
ops.logline_acts
registry.entities
registry.links
audit views
mini_llms.runtime_observations
mini_llms.logline_candidates
Evidence Registry
Ghost Registry
Receipt Registry
Current State
LAB Heartbeat Log
Work Request Ledger
```

Rules:

```txt
Database projection is not authority.
Semantic database writes require LogLine-shaped acts.
Hermes output may be evidence input.
Hermes output may not directly mutate semantic state without admitted projection path.
```

---

## 18. Relationship to mini-llms.rs

mini-llms.rs may be invoked by a Hermes workorder when local/private inference is the task.

Allowed Hermes mini-LLM jobs:

```txt
classify events
extract LogLineCandidate
summarize source packet
detect ghosts
suggest probes
produce Finding / GhostCandidate / DecisionRequest projections
evaluate profile samples
```

Forbidden Hermes mini-LLM jobs:

```txt
approve protected action
execute shell through model output
close receipt
promote canon
write semantic state directly
call model generation evidence
```

If mini-llms.rs returns:

```txt
ReasoningOnlyNoContent
```

Hermes must report it as observation, not failure theater and not candidate success.

---

## 19. Relationship to Process Catalog

Every executable process must point to this contract.

Process entries must declare:

```txt
dispatch required?
Hermes allowed?
mode default?
target LAB?
authority class?
evidence return?
closure path?
ghosts if missing?
```

A process without Hermes boundary must not accidentally become executable.

---

## 20. Relationship to Morning State

Morning State may report Hermes state:

```txt
pending workorders
last executions
failed/inconclusive runs
open Hermes ghosts
evidence returned
receipt candidates pending
LAB availability
```

Morning State may not say:

```txt
Hermes completed the system
Hermes verified the claim
Hermes closed receipt
```

unless receipts or scoped evidence support the exact claim.

---

## 21. Minimal First Vertical Slice

First lawful Hermes slice:

```txt
Process: LAB health check
Dispatch: verification/read-only packet
Admission: dry-run/read-only
Authority: normal, no protected command
Hermes Workorder: run harmless runtime observation
LAB: declared target
Evidence: command output / timestamp / redaction flag
Receipt: none unless scoped receipt path exists
Projection: Current State + Ghost Registry
```

Success criteria:

```txt
workorder accepted
command attempted or ghosted honestly
secret values not printed
evidence returned or missing evidence ghosted
no receipt closure claimed
Current State updated only as projection
```

---

## 22. Implementation Phases

### Phase 0 — Manual Dispatch

Dan manually executes work described by dispatch packets.

Hermes contract is used as checklist.

### Phase 1 — Hermes Dry-Run Worker

Hermes accepts only read-only and dry-run workorders.

No provider mutation, DB semantic write, deploy, route, or public action.

### Phase 2 — Evidence Store

Hermes writes evidence records or exports evidence packets through admitted path.

### Phase 3 — Verification / Build Jobs

Hermes runs tests, builds, schema validation, conformance checks.

### Phase 4 — Limited Apply

Apply mode allowed only with Authority, Dan approval, ExecutionWindow, rollback/rectify path, and receipt profile.

### Phase 5 — App Park Integration

Hermes becomes execution hand for admitted App Park operations.

No App Park deploy without App Park admission.

---

## 23. Security Rules

```txt
No secret values in workorders.
No secret values in logs.
No secret values in reports.
No secret values in receipts.
No secret values in browser payloads.
No env dump.
Secret names may appear when allowed.
Secret presence may be checked.
Secret value inspection is forbidden.
```

Hermes must redact before persistence.

If redaction cannot be guaranteed:

```txt
ghost: secret-redaction-unverified
```

---

## 24. Open Ghosts

```txt
hermes-runtime-not-implemented
hermes-workorder-schema-not-promoted
hermes-execution-report-schema-not-promoted
worker-bridge-absent
lab-inventory-missing
lab-heartbeat-missing
lab-power-state-unknown
host-runtime-unobserved
evidence-store-missing
receipt-registry-missing
execution-window-path-missing
hermes-secret-redaction-unverified
current-state-projection-path-unverified
```

---

## 25. Acceptance Criteria

This contract is accepted when:

```txt
1. Dan promotes or amends it.
2. Dispatch packets reference this contract.
3. Process Catalog entries declare Hermes boundary.
4. 09 Vertical Runtime Doctrine references this contract.
5. Hermes Workorder schema exists or is explicitly ghosted.
6. Hermes Execution Report schema exists or is explicitly ghosted.
7. First read-only/dry-run LAB probe is run or ghosted honestly.
8. Returned evidence is preserved without receipt overclaim.
9. Current State can display Hermes/LAB ghosts.
```

---

## 26. Final Formulation

```txt
Hermes is not the institution.
Hermes is the hand.

A hand does not decide what should be done.
A hand performs admitted work.
A hand returns traces.
A hand does not turn traces into proof.

Minilab decides through runtime and authority.
Hermes executes through workorders.
LABs provide body.
Evidence returns from reality.
Receipts close scope.
Ghosts keep the system honest.
Dan signs consequence.
```

Portuguese:

```txt
Hermes não é a instituição.
Hermes é a mão.

A mão não decide o que deve ser feito.
A mão executa trabalho admitido.
A mão devolve rastros.
A mão não transforma rastros em prova.

Minilab decide por runtime e autoridade.
Hermes executa por workorders.
LABs dão corpo.
Evidência volta da realidade.
Receipts fecham escopo.
Ghosts mantêm o sistema honesto.
Dan assina consequência.
```

Feito — montei o draft **10 — Hermes Dispatch and Execution Contract**.

Ele fecha a costura:

```txt
Process Catalog
→ Vertical Runtime Doctrine
→ Dispatch Packet
→ Authority classification
→ Hermes Workorder
→ LAB execution
→ Execution Report
→ Evidence Record
→ Receipt Candidate or Ghost
→ Current State projection
```

A tese central ficou:

```txt
Dispatch describes.
Runtime admits.
Authority gates.
Hermes executes.
Evidence returns.
Receipts close.
Ghosts preserve.
```

E a formulação de pedra:

```txt
Hermes não é a instituição.
Hermes é a mão.

A mão não decide o que deve ser feito.
A mão executa trabalho admitido.
A mão devolve rastros.
A mão não transforma rastros em prova.
```

Também incluí a parte que você tinha nomeado antes: energia elétrica, máquina acordada, LAB vivo, power/wakefulness e `worker-bridge` como pré-condições materiais — mas sem deixar isso virar autoridade. A frase ficou: **Electricity makes execution possible. It does not make execution permitted.**

Agora o trio está fechado:

```txt
08 — Process Catalog
09 — Vertical Runtime Doctrine
10 — Hermes Dispatch and Execution Contract
```

Próximo passo natural: voltar no **08 Process Catalog** e adicionar o bloco `runtime_dynamics` em cada processo.

**08 Minilab Process Catalog**

# 08 — Minilab Process Catalog

**Status:** canon candidate / operational process draft  
**Layer:** Minilab operational processes, rites, runbooks, vertical runtime entry points  
**Parents:** 01 — Minilab Founding Act; 02 — Organs and Jurisdictions; 03 — Source of Truth Map; 04 — LLM Offices; 05 — Morning State Ritual; 06 — Current State; 07 — Ghost Registry; 09 — Vertical Runtime Doctrine; 10 — Hermes Dispatch and Execution Contract  
**Evidence status:** process-catalog converted from v0.1; runtime-unverified  
**Runtime mutation:** none  
**World-touch:** none

---

## 0. Purpose

This document defines Minilab's operational process catalog.

It is not a five-line path file.  
It is the first operational grammar for how Minilab behaves repeatedly.

A process is a reusable constitutional trajectory. It names what triggers the process, who or which office conducts it, which sources govern it, which steps are allowed, what evidence is required, what can fail, what ghosts may appear, and which process follows.

This catalog exists so future work does not begin from improvisation, mood, scattered chats, or LLM confidence.

---

## 1. Catalog Law

```txt
Processes are how Minilab repeats itself without becoming mechanical fiction.
```

Every process must preserve the distinction between:

```txt
intent
candidate
plan
admission
authority
execution
observation
evidence
receipt
ghost
projection
```

A process may be simple.  
A process may be manual.  
A process may be incomplete.  
A process may be bootstrap-only.

But a process may not hide:

```txt
missing evidence
missing source
missing authority
missing runtime
missing receipt path
missing Dan decision
```

---

## 2. Standard Process Shape

Every process follows this mold:

```yaml
process_id:
name:
family:
status:
trigger:
primary_actor:
primary_office:
preconditions:
steps:
result:
expected_evidence:
failure_modes:
next_process:
runtime_dynamics:
  organ:
  jurisdiction:
  supporting_offices:
  operator_role:
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed: []
    forbidden: []
  model_output_contract:
  candidate_type:
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks: []
    possible_outcomes: []
  authority_boundary:
    class:
    dan_required:
    execution_window_required:
  dispatch_boundary:
    required:
    packet_type:
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed:
    mode:
    target_lab:
  evidence_return:
    required: []
  projection_target: []
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed:
    receipt_profile:
  ghost_path:
    if_missing: []
```

If a process does not need a specific runtime layer, it must say so.

Silence is not a boundary.

---

## 3. Family A — Individual Acts / Writing the World

Family A covers the smallest unit of institutional writing: recording that something exists, happened, was proposed, was observed, was closed, or must remain ghost.

---

### A1 — Write Trivial Personal Act

```yaml
process_id: A1
name: Write trivial personal act
family: individual_acts
status: bootstrap_manual
```

**Trigger**  
Dan wants to record something that happened in life or work: slept, ate, read, finished a task, noticed something, completed a small routine.

**Primary actor**  
Dan.

**Primary office**  
None required. If assisted, Routing Clerk or Morning Scribe.

**Preconditions**

```txt
A current writable act substrate exists, or Dan records the act in the current Cockpit.
If database-backed: ops.logline_acts exists.
```

**Steps**

1. State the act plainly.
2. Reduce it to nine-slot shape if the substrate requires it.
3. Mark evidence state honestly.
4. Record the act.
5. Do not call it receipt unless receipt path exists.

**Result**

```txt
A trivial act is recorded.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
Dan's declaration or direct observation.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
act too trivial for ceremony
schema too strict for bootstrap
LLM over-formalizes trivial life event
act falsely marked verified
```

**Next process**

```txt
A2 if LLM assistance is needed.
A3 if formal receipt is needed.
A4 if act is consequential.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Registry / Estado
  jurisdiction: Cockpit or future ops.logline_acts
  supporting_offices:
    - Morning Scribe if part of daily report
    - Ghost Keeper if evidence is missing
  operator_role: record simple declared state without overclaim
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - shape into nine-slot act
      - suggest evidence_state
    forbidden:
      - mark verified
      - invent evidence
  model_output_contract: LogLineCandidate if model is used
  candidate_type: trivial_act_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - nine-slot shape when formalized
      - status not overclaiming
      - evidence_state declared
    possible_outcomes:
      - admissible_as_bootstrap_act
      - ghost_evidence_missing
  authority_boundary:
    class: none or normal
    dan_required: Dan is actor
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: false
    packet_type: none
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: false
    mode: none
    target_lab: none
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - declaration or observation
  projection_target:
    - Current State if operationally relevant
    - ops.logline_acts when available
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: false by default
    receipt_profile: none
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - act-source-missing
```

---

### A2 — Write Act via LLM Assistance

```yaml
process_id: A2
name: Write act via LLM assistance
family: individual_acts
status: bootstrap_manual
```

**Trigger**  
Dan describes in natural language that something should be recorded.

**Primary actor**  
LLM proposes. Dan reviews and executes/publishes.

**Primary office**  
Routing Clerk or Canon Librarian, depending on scope.

**Preconditions**

```txt
LLM session is inside a known jurisdiction.
Governing source or process is known.
Dan reviews before durable write.
```

**Steps**

1. Dan states the intended act in natural language.
2. LLM proposes nine-slot candidate.
3. LLM marks evidence state without pretending model generation is evidence.
4. LLM presents candidate and any storage/write instruction separately.
5. Dan approves, amends, or rejects.
6. If approved, act is recorded by admitted path.

**Result**

```txt
A reviewed LogLine-shaped act candidate is recorded or rejected.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
Dan review and source context.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
LLM invents hash
LLM treats itself as confirmed_by evidence
LLM proposes status verified/closed
LLM routes to wrong jurisdiction
```

**Next process**

```txt
A3 if receipt needed.
A4 if consequential.
E4 if LLM drifts outside path.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Cockpit
  jurisdiction: active Project / source jurisdiction
  supporting_offices:
    - Canon Librarian
    - Ghost Keeper
  operator_role: transform intent into candidate without executing
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - produce LogLineCandidate
      - detect missing evidence
      - suggest if_doubt path
    forbidden:
      - compute fake hashes
      - claim receipt closure
      - mark itself as evidence
  model_output_contract: LogLineCandidate
  candidate_type: act_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - all nine slots present
      - confirmed_by does not cite model as proof
      - missing evidence routes to if_doubt
      - forbidden closure labels absent
    possible_outcomes:
      - admissible_for_dan_review
      - ghost_evidence_missing
      - reject_overclaim
  authority_boundary:
    class: normal unless consequential
    dan_required: true for durable write
    execution_window_required: false unless consequential execution
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: false unless work crosses into execution/mutation packet
    packet_type: none | mutation
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: false by default
    mode: none
    target_lab: none
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - reviewed candidate
      - Dan approval if written
  projection_target:
    - ops.logline_acts
    - Current State if relevant
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: false by default
    receipt_profile: none
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - llm-candidate-overclaim
      - confirmed-by-evidence-missing
```

---

### A3 — Emit Formal Receipt for Existing Act

```yaml
process_id: A3
name: Emit formal receipt for existing act
family: individual_acts
status: future_formal
```

**Trigger**  
An existing act must become a citable, scoped receipt.

**Primary actor**  
Receipt Reviewer, with Dan review when consequential.

**Primary office**  
Receipt Reviewer.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Act exists.
Receipt profile exists.
Evidence refs exist.
Conformance path exists or ghost is carried.
```

**Steps**

1. Select the act.
2. Confirm the claim and scope.
3. Confirm evidence refs.
4. Build receipt candidate.
5. Run conformance verifier if available.
6. If conformance passes and scope is correct, store/index receipt.
7. If not, open or carry ghost.

**Result**

```txt
Receipt is emitted and indexed, or closure is ghosted/rejected.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
Existing act, evidence refs, conformance result, receipt content hash.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
receipt path missing
conformance unobserved
broad claim from narrow evidence
hash semantics unclear
```

**Next process**

```txt
A5 if receipt affects registry projection.
B3 to read receipts.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Evidence / Receipts / Ghosts
  jurisdiction: Receipts & Ghosts
  supporting_offices:
    - Ghost Keeper
    - Authority Clerk if consequence-bearing
  operator_role: compare claim, scope, evidence, conformance
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - summarize evidence refs
      - detect overclaim
      - draft receipt review note
    forbidden:
      - create receipt by prose
      - validate hash visually
      - close missing evidence
  model_output_contract: Receipt Review draft or LogLineCandidate for review act
  candidate_type: receipt_candidate_review
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - scope explicit
      - evidence refs present
      - conformance status explicit
      - receipt profile named
    possible_outcomes:
      - admissible_for_conformance
      - ghost_conformance_unobserved
      - reject_overclaim
  authority_boundary:
    class: protected if receipt affects consequence
    dan_required: depends on scope
    execution_window_required: false unless verifier run requires runtime execution
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: true if conformance/probe command must run
    packet_type: verification
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true for admitted conformance run
    mode: read_only
    target_lab: verification runtime
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - conformance output
      - receipt hash refs
      - evidence refs
  projection_target:
    - Receipt Registry
    - ops.receipt_index
    - Current State
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: true
    receipt_profile: Foundation-conformant receipt profile
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - receipt-registry-missing
      - conformance-unobserved
      - evidence-registry-missing
```

---

### A4 — Consequential Act with Manual Gate

```yaml
process_id: A4
name: Consequential act with manual gate
family: individual_acts
status: bootstrap_manual
```

**Trigger**  
An act changes the external world: deployment, spending, public communication, provider mutation, database semantic write, authority change, publication, or irreversible operation.

**Primary actor**  
Dan.

**Primary office**  
Authority Clerk.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Candidate act exists.
Risk/blast radius/rollback are stated.
Dan reviews manually.
```

**Steps**

1. State intended effect.
2. State blast radius.
3. State rollback or rectify path.
4. Wait or perform manual review according to gate rule.
5. Dan approves, rejects, or ghosts.
6. If approved, execute through admitted path.
7. Capture evidence.
8. Prepare receipt candidate only if evidence and profile exist.

**Result**

```txt
Consequential action is admitted and executed, rejected, or ghosted.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
Dan approval, execution evidence, rollback/rectify path.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
manual gate skipped
approval ambiguous
execution claimed without evidence
rollback absent
```

**Next process**

```txt
A3 for receipt candidate.
10 Hermes Workorder path if machine execution required.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Authority
  jurisdiction: Authority / Cockpit
  supporting_offices:
    - Ghost Keeper
    - Receipt Reviewer
  operator_role: prepare protected decision without impersonating Dan
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - summarize risk
      - identify missing evidence
      - draft authority packet
    forbidden:
      - approve action
      - open execution window
      - sign consequence
  model_output_contract: Authority Packet draft or LogLineCandidate
  candidate_type: consequential_act_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - effect explicit
      - risk class explicit
      - rollback_or_rectify explicit
      - Dan approval requirement explicit
    possible_outcomes:
      - requires_dan
      - requires_execution_window
      - ghost_authority_path_missing
      - rejected
  authority_boundary:
    class: protected
    dan_required: true
    execution_window_required: depends on command class
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: true if execution/mutation/publication required
    packet_type: mutation | publication | executable
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true only if admitted workorder exists
    mode: dry_run | apply
    target_lab: declared if machine execution
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - approval record
      - execution observation
      - artifact/output refs
  projection_target:
    - Authority Ledger
    - Current State
    - Ghost Registry
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: true after evidence
    receipt_profile: relevant scoped receipt profile
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - dan-approval-missing
      - execution-window-missing
      - rollback-path-missing
      - evidence-return-missing
```

---

### A5 — Project Act into Registry

```yaml
process_id: A5
name: Project act into registry.entities / registry.links
family: individual_acts
status: future_projection
```

**Trigger**  
An act registers, modifies, links, retires, or supersedes a named entity.

**Primary actor**  
Registry / Estado projection path.

**Primary office**  
Canon Librarian or Registry Clerk.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Source act exists.
Projection rule exists.
Entity identity rules are known.
```

**Steps**

1. Identify affected entity/relation.
2. Confirm source act and evidence status.
3. Project insert/update/retire into registry.
4. Preserve source act reference.
5. If duplicate/conflict exists, ghost instead of overwrite.

**Result**

```txt
Registry projection updated or ghosted.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
Source act ref, projection rule, registry state before/after if applicable.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
duplicate identity
unstable name
missing source act
projection path missing
```

**Next process**

```txt
B4 snapshot if significant.
06 Current State update if operationally relevant.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Registry / Estado
  jurisdiction: Registry projection
  supporting_offices:
    - Ghost Keeper
    - Canon Librarian
  operator_role: project named world state without granting authority
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - detect duplicate names
      - suggest relation kind
      - summarize entity metadata
    forbidden:
      - grant permission
      - silently merge identity
      - invent source act
  model_output_contract: Projection candidate or LogLineCandidate
  candidate_type: registry_projection_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - source act exists
      - projection target known
      - identity stable
      - evidence state preserved
    possible_outcomes:
      - admissible_for_projection
      - ghost_duplicate_identity
      - ghost_source_act_missing
  authority_boundary:
    class: normal unless projection changes protected authority
    dan_required: false unless jurisdiction/source-of-truth changes
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: true if DB mutation executed by Hermes/tool
    packet_type: mutation
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true for admitted projection job
    mode: apply only with projection authority
    target_lab: DB/projection runtime
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - source act ref
      - projection result
  projection_target:
    - registry.entities
    - registry.links
    - Current State
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: false by default
    receipt_profile: none
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - stable-entity-ids-missing
      - projection-path-missing
      - duplicate-identity
```

---

## 4. Family B — Reading and State

Family B covers state visibility: current state, ghosts, receipts, and snapshots.

---

### B1 — Read Today's State

```yaml
process_id: B1
name: Read today's state
family: reading_state
status: bootstrap_manual
```

**Trigger**  
Dan wants to know what is open, what needs action, what changed, what is ghost, or what needs Dan.

**Primary actor**  
Dan or Morning Scribe.

**Primary office**  
Morning Scribe.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Current State exists or bootstrap report exists.
Future: audit view exists.
```

**Steps**

1. Open Current State / Morning State / future audit view.
2. Read overall state.
3. Read ghosts.
4. Identify what needs Dan.
5. Choose next act.

**Result**

```txt
Dan has a current operational view.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
Current State, Ghost Registry, Morning State, or audit view.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
view empty
source stale
state inferred from memory
report treated as receipt
```

**Next process**

```txt
B2 for ghosts.
A1/A2/A4 for action.
G1 for Morning State.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Cockpit
  jurisdiction: Morning State / Current State
  supporting_offices:
    - Ghost Keeper
    - Routing Clerk
  operator_role: render state without inventing proof
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - summarize current state
      - group open ghosts
      - suggest next acts
    forbidden:
      - mark verified
      - invent changes
      - treat memory as source
  model_output_contract: Morning State report or summary; LogLineCandidate only if act recorded
  candidate_type: state_read_report
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - source named
      - evidence states preserved
      - no proof closure claimed
    possible_outcomes:
      - admissible_as_report
      - ghost_current_state_missing
      - ghost_source_stale
  authority_boundary:
    class: read_only
    dan_required: false
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: false
    packet_type: none
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: false unless audit query/probe is delegated
    mode: read_only
    target_lab: none
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - source refs or statement that source is missing
  projection_target:
    - Morning State
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: false
    receipt_profile: none
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - current-state-missing
      - state-stale
      - source-of-truth-unpromoted
```

---

### B2 — Read Open Ghosts

```yaml
process_id: B2
name: Read open ghosts
family: reading_state
status: bootstrap_manual
```

**Trigger**  
Dan or an operator wants to review what prevents honest closure.

**Primary actor**  
Ghost Keeper.

**Primary office**  
Ghost Keeper.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Ghost Registry exists or bootstrap ghost list exists.
```

**Steps**

1. Read open ghosts.
2. Preserve priority and organ.
3. For each important ghost, decide: carry, narrow, close candidate, supersede, retire, or route.
4. Do not close without evidence or Dan-reviewed closure.

**Result**

```txt
Open missing-proof state is visible and routed.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
Ghost Registry, Current State, or act graph projection.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
ghost registry missing
ghosts treated as failures
ghosts closed by explanation
old ghosts ignored
```

**Next process**

```txt
A1/A2 for small act.
A3 for closure candidate.
G3 for weekly review.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Evidence / Receipts / Ghosts
  jurisdiction: Ghost Registry
  supporting_offices:
    - Morning Scribe
    - Routing Clerk
  operator_role: preserve missing proof and route next act
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - cluster ghosts
      - identify stale ghosts
      - suggest smallest next probe
    forbidden:
      - close ghost by explanation
      - convert absence into failure without basis
  model_output_contract: Ghost Review or LogLineCandidate for carry/close act
  candidate_type: ghost_review_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - ghost source known or bootstrap=true
      - closure condition explicit
      - evidence missing preserved
    possible_outcomes:
      - carry_ghost
      - narrow_ghost
      - ghost_registry_missing
      - close_candidate_requires_evidence
  authority_boundary:
    class: read_only
    dan_required: false unless closing consequential ghost
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: false unless probe is requested
    packet_type: verification
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true only if admitted probe workorder follows
    mode: read_only | dry_run
    target_lab: depends on probe
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - ghost source refs
      - missing proof statement
  projection_target:
    - Ghost Registry
    - Morning State
    - Current State
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: only after evidence exists
    receipt_profile: ghost closure profile if defined
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - ghost-registry-missing
      - evidence-registry-missing
```

```yaml
process_id: B3
```

**Expected evidence**

**Failure modes**

```txt
broad interpretation from narrow receipt
```

```txt
Publication or report drafting if scoped claims are needed.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Evidence / Receipts / Ghosts
  jurisdiction: Receipt Registry
  supporting_offices:
    - Canon Librarian
    - Ghost Keeper
  operator_role: read closures without expanding scope
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - summarize receipt scopes
      - detect unsupported broad claims
    forbidden:
      - call candidate a receipt
      - infer production safety
  model_output_contract: Receipt summary; LogLineCandidate only if review act recorded
  candidate_type: receipt_read_report
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - receipt refs exist
      - scope preserved
      - conformance state not invented
    possible_outcomes:
      - admissible_as_read_report
      - ghost_receipt_registry_missing
      - reject_broad_claim
  authority_boundary:
    class: read_only
    dan_required: false
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: false unless verifier/probe requested
    packet_type: verification
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true only for admitted conformance query
    mode: read_only
    target_lab: verification runtime
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - receipt refs
  projection_target:
    - Morning State
    - reports
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: false
    receipt_profile: none
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - receipt-registry-missing
      - conformance-unobserved
```

### B4 — Snapshot Named World

```yaml
process_id: B4
name: Snapshot named world
family: reading_state
status: future_formal
```

**Trigger**  
Weekly/monthly review, before major change, or before migration.

**Primary actor**  
Registry / Estado.

**Primary office**  
Canon Librarian or Archive Keeper.

**Preconditions**

```txt
registry.entities and registry.links exist, or markdown/current state source exists.
```

**Steps**

1. Export current registry world.
2. Hash snapshot.
3. Store snapshot in durable location.
4. Record snapshot act.
5. Project snapshot reference.

**Result**

```txt
Named world snapshot exists and can be referenced.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
snapshot artifact, hash, snapshot act.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
registry storage undecided
snapshot hash missing
snapshot stored but not referenced
```

**Next process**

```txt
G4 monthly snapshot.
Archive review if superseded.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Registry / Estado
  jurisdiction: Registry / Archive
  supporting_offices:
    - Archive Keeper
    - Ghost Keeper
  operator_role: preserve current named world without redefining truth
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - summarize snapshot contents
      - detect missing entity classes
    forbidden:
      - mutate registry
      - declare snapshot canonical by itself
  model_output_contract: Snapshot summary or LogLineCandidate for snapshot act
  candidate_type: snapshot_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - source registry exists
      - storage location declared
      - hash present or ghosted
    possible_outcomes:
      - admissible_snapshot
      - ghost_registry_storage_undecided
      - ghost_snapshot_hash_missing
  authority_boundary:
    class: read_only unless storage mutation is protected
    dan_required: false unless durable canon storage decision changes
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: true if Hermes/export command runs
    packet_type: verification
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true for admitted export/hash job
    mode: read_only
    target_lab: DB/runtime host
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - artifact ref
      - hash
      - export command output if automated
  projection_target:
    - Snapshot Registry
    - Current State
    - Archive
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: true if snapshot needs formal closure
    receipt_profile: minilab.snapshot.receipt_profile.v1
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - registry-storage-undecided
      - snapshot-hash-missing
      - projection-path-missing
```

## 5. Family C — Information Intake

Family C covers how thoughts, files, notes, observations, and uploads enter Minilab without immediately becoming truth.

---

### C1 — Capture Loose Thought

```yaml
process_id: C1
name: Capture loose thought
family: information_intake
status: bootstrap_manual
```

**Trigger**  
Dan has an idea, observation, suspicion, phrase, or reminder that may or may not become work.

**Primary actor**  
Dan.

**Primary office**  
Routing Clerk if assisted.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Inbox jurisdiction exists, or Dan uses current Cockpit.
```

**Steps**

1. Capture the thought with minimal friction.
2. Do not classify deeply yet.
3. Preserve source/context if relevant.
4. Leave for triage.

**Result**

```txt
Thought preserved without premature ceremony.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
Captured note/thread/item.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
inbox becomes permanent workspace
thought treated as plan or truth
lost source context
```

**Next process**

```txt
C2 triage.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Cockpit
  jurisdiction: Inbox
  supporting_offices:
    - Routing Clerk
  operator_role: capture without over-processing
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - lightly summarize if requested
    forbidden:
      - invent project
      - execute work
      - mark as current state
  model_output_contract: none by default
  candidate_type: intake_note
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - not treated as source of truth
      - not treated as execution
    possible_outcomes:
      - captured
      - ghost_inbox_missing
  authority_boundary:
    class: none
    dan_required: false
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: false
    packet_type: none
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: false
    mode: none
    target_lab: none
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - captured item
  projection_target:
    - Inbox
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: false
    receipt_profile: none
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - inbox-jurisdiction-missing
```

---

### C2 — Triage Inbox

```yaml
process_id: C2
name: Triage Inbox
family: information_intake
status: bootstrap_manual
```

**Trigger**  
Inbox has accumulated items.

**Primary actor**  
Routing Clerk / Dan.

**Primary office**  
Routing Clerk.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Inbox items exist.
```

**Steps**

1. Review each item.
2. Classify as act, ghost, routed work, archive, discard, or process gap.
3. Move or reference item in the right jurisdiction.
4. Do not do deep work in Inbox.

**Result**

```txt
Inbox items are routed or retired.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
routing notes, moved items, or discarded items.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
Inbox becomes work room
scope unclear
project assumed before Dan creates it
```

**Next process**

```txt
C3 route item.
A1/A2 write act.
H1 if missing process.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Cockpit
  jurisdiction: Inbox / Routing
  supporting_offices:
    - Ghost Keeper
    - Canon Librarian if doctrine-related
  operator_role: route work to correct organ
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - classify items
      - suggest organ/jurisdiction
      - detect process gaps
    forbidden:
      - create Project
      - silently redefine scope
      - complete deep work in Inbox
  model_output_contract: Routing Note or LogLineCandidate if route act recorded
  candidate_type: routing_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - target organ declared
      - source preserved
      - scope not silently expanded
    possible_outcomes:
      - admissible_route
      - ghost_jurisdiction_unclear
      - project_change_request_needed
  authority_boundary:
    class: normal
    dan_required: true if new jurisdiction requested
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: false unless work unit created
    packet_type: communication | mutation
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: false
    mode: none
    target_lab: none
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - routing decision
  projection_target:
    - Work Request Ledger
    - Current State if relevant
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: false
    receipt_profile: none
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - jurisdiction-unclear
      - owner-missing
      - next-act-missing
```

---

### C3 — Route Item to Proper Project / Jurisdiction

```yaml
process_id: C3
name: Route item to proper Project or jurisdiction
family: information_intake
status: bootstrap_manual
```

**Trigger**  
Triage determines item belongs elsewhere.

**Primary actor**  
Routing Clerk / Dan.

**Primary office**  
Routing Clerk.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Destination jurisdiction exists, or Project Change Request is needed.
```

**Steps**

1. Identify destination organ and jurisdiction.
2. If jurisdiction exists, create/continue thread with constructor.
3. Preserve source item.
4. Mark original item as routed.
5. If destination does not exist, prepare Project Change Request.

**Result**

```txt
Work is moved to correct scope.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
routing note, destination thread/source, original item reference.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
work silently moved
new Project assumed
source lost
```

**Next process**

```txt
Relevant organ process.
Project Change Request if needed.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Cockpit
  jurisdiction: Routing / destination jurisdiction
  supporting_offices:
    - Canon Librarian
    - Ghost Keeper
  operator_role: move work without losing source or scope
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - draft constructor message
      - summarize source item
    forbidden:
      - create Project
      - claim routing as completion
  model_output_contract: Routing Note
  candidate_type: jurisdiction_route_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - destination exists or change request produced
      - source preserved
      - no scope drift
    possible_outcomes:
      - routed
      - needs_project_change_request
      - ghost_destination_missing
  authority_boundary:
    class: normal
    dan_required: true if jurisdiction creation/change
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: false
    packet_type: communication
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: false
    mode: none
    target_lab: none
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - destination reference
  projection_target:
    - Work Request Ledger
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: false
    receipt_profile: none
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - destination-jurisdiction-missing
      - source-context-lost
```

---

### C4 — Receive Uploaded File

```yaml
process_id: C4
name: Receive uploaded file
family: information_intake
status: bootstrap_manual
```

**Trigger**  
A document, screenshot, code file, data file, image, or artifact enters Minilab.

**Primary actor**  
Dan / Canon Librarian / Evidence office depending file class.

**Primary office**  
Canon Librarian or Receipt Reviewer.

**Preconditions**

```txt
File is available.
Classification is required before promotion.
```

**Steps**

1. Classify file as evidence, doctrine candidate, reference, operational source, archive, or discardable.
2. Check for secrets.
3. Decide storage/promotion path.
4. Record source and evidence state.
5. Do not treat uploaded file as canon by default.

**Result**

```txt
File is classified and routed.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
file ref, classification, source class, secret check status.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
file treated as canon
secret uploaded
file used without source class
artifact lost
```

**Next process**

```txt
Canon promotion.
Evidence registry.
Archive.
Receipt review.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Registry / Estado
  jurisdiction: Files / Evidence / Canon depending class
  supporting_offices:
    - Canon Librarian
    - Receipt Reviewer
    - Ghost Keeper
  operator_role: classify file before use
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - summarize file
      - suggest source class
      - detect claims/ghosts
    forbidden:
      - assume file is canonical
      - ignore secret risk
      - mark as receipt
  model_output_contract: File Classification Note or LogLineCandidate if recorded
  candidate_type: file_intake_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - source class assigned
      - secret safety declared
      - evidence state declared
    possible_outcomes:
      - admissible_file_context
      - ghost_secret_scan_missing
      - ghost_source_class_missing
  authority_boundary:
    class: normal; protected if promotion/canon/source-of-truth change
    dan_required: true for promotion
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: true if automated scan/export/store command runs
    packet_type: inspection | mutation
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true for admitted scan/hash/extract job
    mode: read_only
    target_lab: file processing runtime
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - file ref
      - classification
      - secret scan/redaction status when relevant
  projection_target:
    - Source Map
    - Evidence Registry
    - Archive
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: only if file supports scoped claim
    receipt_profile: evidence/file receipt profile if defined
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - file-source-class-missing
      - secret-scan-unverified
      - durable-storage-undecided
```
