## 6. Family D — LAB / Workers / Hermes

Family D covers machine state, power, heartbeat, worker execution, and the path toward Hermes.

---

### D1 — Verify Machine Health

```yaml
process_id: D1
name: Verify machine health
family: lab_workers
status: bootstrap_manual
```

**Trigger**  
Morning State, suspicion that a machine slept/shut down, pre-execution check, or weekly review.

**Primary actor**  
LAB Reporter.

**Primary office**  
LAB Reporter.

**Preconditions**

```txt
LAB Inventory exists or inventory ghost is carried.
Heartbeat source exists or heartbeat ghost is carried.
```

**Steps**

1. Read machine inventory.
2. Read last heartbeat or manual observation.
3. Classify machine state: unknown, alive, stale, offline, degraded.
4. If stale/unknown, open or carry ghost.
5. If work is requested, verify authority path before execution.

**Result**

```txt
LAB health state is visible.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
LAB inventory, heartbeat/manual observation, timestamp.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
no inventory
no heartbeat
machine existence assumed
uptime inferred from hope
```

**Next process**

```txt
D2 if missing.
D3 if investigation needed.
D5 if heartbeat must be built.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: LAB
  jurisdiction: LAB / Morning State
  supporting_offices:
    - Ghost Keeper
    - Authority Clerk if commands are requested
  operator_role: report physical-digital state honestly
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - summarize heartbeat history
      - classify stale/offline/unknown
      - suggest next probe
    forbidden:
      - claim alive without observation
      - authorize commands
      - close receipt
  model_output_contract: LogLineCandidate if local cognition invoked
  candidate_type: lab_health_observation_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - source exists or ghost named
      - evidence state declared
      - no execution claimed from missing heartbeat
    possible_outcomes:
      - admissible_as_report
      - ghost_lab_inventory_missing
      - ghost_lab_heartbeat_missing
      - requires_hermes_probe
  authority_boundary:
    class: read_only for report; executable if probe command requested
    dan_required: false for report; true if protected host action
    execution_window_required: only for protected host command
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: true if automated probe is requested
    packet_type: verification | executable
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true only for admitted probe workorder
    mode: read_only | dry_run
    target_lab: declared LAB
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - heartbeat/manual observation
      - timestamp
      - runtime status output if probed
  projection_target:
    - Current State
    - Ghost Registry
    - Morning State
    - LAB_HEARTBEAT_LOG
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: only after scoped probe
    receipt_profile: minilab.health.receipt_profile.v1
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - lab-inventory-missing
      - lab-heartbeat-missing
      - lab-power-state-unknown
      - host-runtime-unobserved
```

---

### D2 — Ghost Missing Machine / Missing Heartbeat

```yaml
process_id: D2
name: Ghost missing machine or heartbeat
family: lab_workers
status: bootstrap_manual
```

**Trigger**  
A machine has not reported within expected time, or power/runtime state is unknown.

**Primary actor**  
LAB Reporter / Ghost Keeper.

**Primary office**  
Ghost Keeper.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Expected heartbeat or observation cadence exists, or cadence absence is itself ghosted.
```

**Steps**

1. Identify missing machine or heartbeat.
2. Open or carry ghost.
3. State what it blocks.
4. State next check.
5. Do not mark machine dead unless observed.

**Result**

```txt
Missing LAB state is explicit.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
last observation, expected cadence, missing heartbeat condition.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
absence hidden
absence treated as failure without evidence
machine removed without source
```

**Next process**

```txt
D3 investigate.
D5 build heartbeat.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: LAB
  jurisdiction: Ghost Registry / LAB
  supporting_offices:
    - LAB Reporter
    - Morning Scribe
  operator_role: preserve missing machine evidence
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - draft ghost record
      - suggest smallest next observation
    forbidden:
      - infer cause
      - close missing machine state
  model_output_contract: GhostCandidate or LogLineCandidate
  candidate_type: lab_ghost_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - missing condition explicit
      - closure condition explicit
      - no false machine state
    possible_outcomes:
      - open_ghost
      - carry_ghost
      - reject_duplicate_ghost
  authority_boundary:
    class: normal
    dan_required: false unless physical action needed
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: false unless investigation job requested
    packet_type: verification
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true only for admitted remote probe
    mode: read_only
    target_lab: affected or observer LAB
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - missing condition
      - last observed timestamp if available
  projection_target:
    - Ghost Registry
    - Current State
    - Morning State
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: false until observation exists
    receipt_profile: none
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - lab-heartbeat-missing
      - lab-power-state-unknown
      - host-runtime-unobserved
```

---

### D3 — Investigate Silent LAB

```yaml
process_id: D3
name: Investigate silent LAB
family: lab_workers
status: manual_physical
```

**Trigger**  
A LAB ghost indicates stale/offline/unknown state.

**Primary actor**  
Dan physically or admitted remote probe.

**Primary office**  
LAB Reporter.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Ghost exists.
Physical or remote observation is possible.
```

**Steps**

1. Attempt physical check, ping, SSH, or admitted probe.
2. Identify cause if observable.
3. Restore if safe and authorized.
4. Record observation.
5. Close or narrow ghost only within evidence scope.

**Result**

```txt
LAB state is observed, restored, or remains ghost.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
manual observation, ping/SSH output, power state, process status.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
physical action unrecorded
remote command without authority
restore claimed without evidence
```

**Next process**

```txt
D1 verify again.
D5 if heartbeat absent.
A3 if scoped receipt needed.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: LAB
  jurisdiction: LAB / Physical site / Hermes if remote
  supporting_offices:
    - Authority Clerk
    - Ghost Keeper
  operator_role: investigate missing LAB without inventing cause
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - summarize possible causes after evidence
      - draft recovery checklist
    forbidden:
      - execute commands
      - infer cause without observation
  model_output_contract: LAB Report or LogLineCandidate
  candidate_type: lab_investigation_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - investigation scope explicit
      - command class classified if remote
      - evidence state declared
    possible_outcomes:
      - manual_observation_admissible
      - requires_hermes_probe
      - requires_dan_physical_action
      - ghost_unreachable
  authority_boundary:
    class: normal for manual observation; protected for host mutation
    dan_required: true for physical/protected action
    execution_window_required: if protected command
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: true for remote command/probe
    packet_type: verification | executable
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true for admitted read-only probe
    mode: read_only | dry_run
    target_lab: affected LAB or observer host
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - observation output
      - cause if known
      - action taken if any
  projection_target:
    - LAB_HEALTH_RECORDS
    - Ghost Registry
    - Current State
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: only for scoped restored/observed claim
    receipt_profile: minilab.lab_observation.receipt_profile.v1
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - lab-physical-access-missing
      - remote-access-unavailable
      - restore-evidence-missing
```

---

### D4 — Submit Worker Job Request

```yaml
process_id: D4
name: Submit worker job request
family: lab_workers
status: transitional_to_hermes
```

**Trigger**  
A machine should perform expensive or local work: inference, media processing, embeddings, build/test, verification, artifact generation.

**Primary actor**  
Operator prepares; Authority admits; Hermes executes when available.

**Primary office**  
Authority Clerk + LAB Reporter.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Target LAB declared.
Work scope explicit.
Evidence required.
Authority class known.
```

**Steps**

1. Prepare Worker Job Request / Dispatch Packet.
2. Classify authority and risk.
3. Admit or ghost through Constitutional Runtime / Authority.
4. If no bridge exists, execute manually or carry bridge ghost.
5. Capture evidence.
6. Return execution report.

**Result**

```txt
Worker job executes, is manually run, or is ghosted.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
work request, approval if needed, stdout/stderr/artifacts, execution report.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
worker bridge absent
job executes without admitted scope
evidence missing
secret leakage
```

**Next process**

```txt
10 Hermes Workorder path.
A3 if receipt candidate needed.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: LAB
  jurisdiction: Worker Fleet / Hermes
  supporting_offices:
    - Authority Clerk
    - Receipt Reviewer
    - Ghost Keeper
  operator_role: prepare bounded work without executing from language
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - draft workorder
      - classify expected evidence
      - suggest target LAB based on declared capabilities
    forbidden:
      - choose protected execution by itself
      - embed secret values
      - claim execution
  model_output_contract: Dispatch Packet / LogLineCandidate
  candidate_type: worker_job_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - target LAB declared
      - allowed/forbidden actions explicit
      - evidence required
      - mode explicit
    possible_outcomes:
      - admit_for_dispatch
      - requires_authority
      - ghost_worker_bridge_absent
      - reject_unbounded_job
  authority_boundary:
    class: executable
    dan_required: depends on risk/protected class
    execution_window_required: for protected/apply jobs
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: true
    packet_type: executable
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true after admission
    mode: read_only | dry_run | apply
    target_lab: declared LAB
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - execution report
      - stdout/stderr refs
      - artifact hashes
      - secret_redacted=true
  projection_target:
    - Work Request Ledger
    - Evidence Registry
    - Current State
    - Ghost Registry
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: after evidence
    receipt_profile: minilab.command.receipt_profile.v1
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - worker-bridge-absent
      - target-lab-missing
      - evidence-return-missing
      - secret-policy-missing
```

---

### D5 — Machine Heartbeat

```yaml
process_id: D5
name: Machine heartbeat
family: lab_workers
status: to_build
```

**Trigger**  
A LAB machine periodically reports that it is alive.

**Primary actor**  
Daemon / Hermes / future worker agent.

**Primary office**  
LAB Reporter.

**Preconditions**

```txt
LAB identity exists.
Heartbeat target exists.
Secret policy configured.
```

**Steps**

1. Machine emits heartbeat act or observation.
2. Store heartbeat in declared substrate.
3. Project latest heartbeat to LAB state.
4. Morning State reads freshness.
5. Missing heartbeat opens/carries ghost.

**Result**

```txt
LAB liveness becomes observable over time.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
heartbeat timestamp, lab_id, runtime id, redacted payload.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
heartbeat daemon not built
machine sleeps
network unavailable
heartbeat treated as authority
```

**Next process**

```txt
D1 health check.
D2 ghost if missing.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: LAB
  jurisdiction: LAB_HEARTBEAT_LOG / Hermes
  supporting_offices:
    - Ghost Keeper
    - Authority Clerk if daemon installation is needed
  operator_role: maintain observable liveness without granting power
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - summarize heartbeat trends
      - detect stale heartbeats
    forbidden:
      - claim authorization
      - hide stale state
  model_output_contract: none for daemon; LogLineCandidate for heartbeat act if generated
  candidate_type: heartbeat_observation
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - lab identity stable
      - heartbeat shape valid
      - no secret values
      - projection target declared
    possible_outcomes:
      - admissible_heartbeat
      - ghost_lab_identity_missing
      - ghost_heartbeat_path_missing
  authority_boundary:
    class: normal for heartbeat; protected for daemon install
    dan_required: true for install/config change
    execution_window_required: if protected host command
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: true for daemon install/build
    packet_type: code | executable
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true for admitted heartbeat daemon/probe
    mode: read_only | apply for install only with authority
    target_lab: each LAB
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - heartbeat payload
      - timestamp
      - redaction status
  projection_target:
    - LAB_HEARTBEAT_LOG
    - Current State
    - Morning State
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: only for scoped heartbeat probe/install
    receipt_profile: minilab.heartbeat.receipt_profile.v1
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - heartbeat-daemon-missing
      - lab-sleep-prevention-unverified
      - lab-power-state-unknown
```

## 7. Family E — Work with LLMs

Family E governs model assistance in Minilab.

---

### E1 — Start LLM Conversation

```yaml
process_id: E1
name: Start LLM conversation
family: llm_work
status: bootstrap_manual
```

**Trigger**  
Dan wants LLM help for a specific task.

**Primary actor**  
Dan.

**Primary office**  
Depends on task; Routing Clerk if unclear.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Jurisdiction is selected.
Office mandate is known.
Relevant sources are mounted or named.
```

**Steps**

1. Identify correct Project/jurisdiction.
2. Start conversation with constructor context.
3. State office or expected role.
4. Provide task and sources.
5. Require handoff with status/evidence/ghosts/next act.

**Result**

```txt
LLM operates inside office scope.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
chat context, source refs, handoff.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
LLM chooses its own role
wrong jurisdiction
memory treated as source
scope expands silently
```

**Next process**

```txt
E2 if act proposed.
E3 if doctrine change proposed.
E4 if drift.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Cockpit
  jurisdiction: selected Project / office
  supporting_offices:
    - Routing Clerk
    - Canon Librarian if doctrine
  operator_role: occupy office under mandate
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - assist within declared task
    forbidden:
      - create jurisdiction
      - claim execution
      - close proof
  model_output_contract: office-specific handoff; LogLineCandidate if act proposed
  candidate_type: operator_session
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - office declared
      - source refs named
      - handoff required
    possible_outcomes:
      - admissible_operator_session
      - ghost_office_missing
      - ghost_source_missing
  authority_boundary:
    class: advisory
    dan_required: false unless promotion/authority requested
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: false unless work unit created
    packet_type: none
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: false
    mode: none
    target_lab: none
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - handoff
  projection_target:
    - Work Request Ledger if task tracked
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: false
    receipt_profile: none
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - office-missing-for-session
      - source-not-mounted
      - handoff-missing
```

---

### E2 — LLM Proposes Act

```yaml
process_id: E2
name: LLM proposes act
family: llm_work
status: bootstrap_manual
```

**Trigger**  
A model suggests a LogLine-shaped act, database write, projection, or candidate.

**Primary actor**  
LLM proposes. Dan/operator reviews.

**Primary office**  
Depends on organ; Canon Librarian or Routing Clerk if ambiguous.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Office and source are known.
Model output is candidate only.
```

**Steps**

1. Generate candidate act.
2. Confirm nine slots.
3. Confirm evidence state.
4. Reject false closure labels.
5. Route to Dan/admission/write path.

**Result**

```txt
Candidate is accepted for review, amended, rejected, or ghosted.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
candidate, source context, review decision.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
fake hash
model as confirmed_by proof
overclaim
wrong source class
```

**Next process**

```txt
A2 write via LLM.
A4 if consequential.
E4 if drift.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: depends on target act
  jurisdiction: active office
  supporting_offices:
    - Ghost Keeper
    - Receipt Reviewer if closure implied
  operator_role: review candidate, not execute it
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - propose candidate
      - identify missing evidence
    forbidden:
      - admit its own act
      - claim truth
  model_output_contract: LogLineCandidate
  candidate_type: model_act_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - all nine slots
      - confirmed_by evidence path valid
      - if_doubt handles missing evidence
      - status candidate/draft unless supported
    possible_outcomes:
      - admissible_for_review
      - guard_rejected
      - ghost_evidence_missing
  authority_boundary:
    class: normal unless consequential
    dan_required: true for durable write/promotion/protected action
    execution_window_required: depends on consequence
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: if action crosses into work unit
    packet_type: mutation | executable | communication
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: only if dispatch admitted
    mode: dry_run | apply
    target_lab: declared if execution
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - review decision
  projection_target:
    - ops.logline_acts if written
    - Current State if relevant
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: false by default
    receipt_profile: none
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - model-output-overclaim
      - confirmed-by-evidence-missing
```

---

### E3 — LLM Proposes Doctrine Change

```yaml
process_id: E3
name: LLM proposes doctrine change
family: llm_work
status: bootstrap_manual
```

**Trigger**  
A model identifies contradiction, lacuna, or improvement in doctrine.

**Primary actor**  
LLM drafts. Canon Librarian reviews. Dan promotes.

**Primary office**  
Canon Librarian.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Affected document/source named.
Change is a proposal, not canon.
```

**Steps**

1. Draft change as diff or amendment candidate.
2. Identify what it supersedes or modifies.
3. Identify risks and ghosts.
4. Dan reviews.
5. Promote, reject, or archive.

**Result**

```txt
Doctrine change candidate exists.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
diff, rationale, affected sources, Dan decision for promotion.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
model rewrites canon silently
source hierarchy ignored
beauty promoted without evidence
```

**Next process**

```txt
F1 propose canon change.
Promotion Record.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Constitution
  jurisdiction: Canon / docs
  supporting_offices:
    - Ghost Keeper
    - Research Registrar if research-based
  operator_role: prepare amendment without promotion authority
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - draft diff
      - identify conflicts
      - summarize rationale
    forbidden:
      - promote canon
      - rewrite parent canon locally
      - hide supersession
  model_output_contract: Canon Note / amendment draft
  candidate_type: doctrine_change_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - source document named
      - status candidate
      - promotion authority explicit
      - conflict/ghost list present
    possible_outcomes:
      - candidate_for_dan_review
      - ghost_promotion_record_missing
      - reject_conflict_with_parent_canon
  authority_boundary:
    class: protected for canon promotion
    dan_required: true
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: true if file/repo mutation requested
    packet_type: mutation | code
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true only for admitted docs build/check
    mode: dry_run | apply with Dan approval
    target_lab: docs runtime
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - diff
      - review decision
      - build/check output if run
  projection_target:
    - Source of Truth Map
    - Archive
    - Current State
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: if promoted and receipt path exists
    receipt_profile: minilab.doctrine.receipt_profile.v1
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - promotion-record-missing
      - canon-conflict-unresolved
      - durable-canon-storage-undecided
```

### E4 — LLM Suggests Path Outside Rails

```yaml
process_id: E4
name: LLM suggests path outside rails
family: llm_work
status: active_guardrail
```

**Trigger**  
LLM proposes architecture, action, authority, execution, or scope outside declared paths.

**Primary actor**  
Dan/operator stops the session.

**Primary office**  
Routing Clerk or Canon Librarian.

**Preconditions**

```txt
A declared path or source map exists.
```

**Steps**

1. Interrupt the path.
2. State which boundary was crossed.
3. Redirect to existing path or open process-gap ghost.
4. End session if drift persists.

**Result**

```txt
Institutional rails are preserved.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
drift statement, correction, ghost if needed.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
operator follows attractive drift
new architecture invented unnecessarily
scope expands silently
```

**Next process**

```txt
H1 if process missing.
C3 route.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Cockpit
  jurisdiction: active session
  supporting_offices:
    - Ghost Keeper
    - Canon Librarian
  operator_role: stop drift and preserve mandate
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - explain alternative path if asked
    forbidden:
      - continue unsupported architecture
  model_output_contract: Drift Correction Note
  candidate_type: drift_guard_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - violated boundary named
      - existing path proposed or ghost opened
    possible_outcomes:
      - route_to_existing_process
      - open_process_gap
      - end_session
  authority_boundary:
    class: normal
    dan_required: false unless new jurisdiction/canon requested
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: false
    packet_type: none
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: false
    mode: none
    target_lab: none
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - drift note
  projection_target:
    - Ghost Registry if repeated
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: false
    receipt_profile: none
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - process-path-missing
      - operator-scope-drift
```

---

### E5 — LLM Reviews Work from Another LLM

```yaml
process_id: E5
name: LLM reviews work from another LLM
family: llm_work
status: bootstrap_manual
```

**Trigger**  
Important output from one model needs adversarial or second-pass review.

**Primary actor**  
Dan initiates. Second model reviews.

**Primary office**  
Relevant office; Receipt Reviewer or Canon Librarian if proof/doctrine.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Original proposal and sources are provided.
Review model is told scope and criteria.
```

**Steps**

1. Provide original proposal.
2. Provide governing sources.
3. Ask for critique, missing evidence, overclaim, and ghosts.
4. Compare outputs.
5. Dan/operator decides.

**Result**

```txt
LLM proposal is stress-tested.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
review note, disagreement list, ghosts.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
second LLM amplifies first overclaim
review lacks source refs
confidence mistaken for proof
```

**Next process**

```txt
A2/A3/E3/F1 depending outcome.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: depends on target
  jurisdiction: review session
  supporting_offices:
    - Ghost Keeper
    - Receipt Reviewer
  operator_role: adversarial review under source discipline
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - critique output
      - detect overclaim
      - propose missing probes
    forbidden:
      - settle truth without evidence
      - close disagreement by consensus
  model_output_contract: Review Note
  candidate_type: llm_review_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - source refs included
      - evidence state preserved
      - disagreements named
    possible_outcomes:
      - review_admissible
      - ghost_source_missing
      - reject_unreviewable_output
  authority_boundary:
    class: advisory
    dan_required: if final decision consequential
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: false unless probe/work requested
    packet_type: verification
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true only for admitted verification job
    mode: read_only
    target_lab: verification runtime
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - review note
  projection_target:
    - Work Request Ledger if tracked
    - Ghost Registry if issues found
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: false
    receipt_profile: none
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - review-source-missing
      - unresolved-model-disagreement
```

## 8. Family F — Governance and Change

Family F governs canon, doctrine, errata, retirement, and promoted institutional changes.

---

### F1 — Propose Canon Change

```yaml
process_id: F1
name: Propose canon change
family: governance_change
status: future_formal
```

**Trigger**  
A normative change is needed in LogLine Foundation or Minilab canon.

**Primary actor**  
Dan / Canon Librarian / Governance Scribe.

**Primary office**  
Canon Librarian.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Affected canon identified.
Change is scoped.
Promotion path exists.
```

**Steps**

1. Draft LIP/amendment/governance note.
2. Mark status Draft.
3. State motivation, scope, compatibility, ghosts.
4. Review.
5. Promote, reject, or supersede.
6. Implement downstream if accepted.

**Result**

```txt
Canon change is proposed through governance path.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
draft, review, decision, accepted/rejected status.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
local shortcut becomes law
parent canon redefined locally
promotion record missing
```

**Next process**

```txt
E3 for LLM-aided draft.
Promotion Record.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Constitution
  jurisdiction: governance / doctrine source
  supporting_offices:
    - Ghost Keeper
    - Research Registrar if experiment-derived
  operator_role: propose law without bypassing governance
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - draft amendment
      - find conflicts
      - summarize compatibility
    forbidden:
      - accept amendment
      - rewrite parent canon by local fiat
  model_output_contract: Governance Note / LogLineCandidate for proposal act
  candidate_type: canon_change_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - affected source named
      - normative change explicit
      - status draft/proposed
      - promotion authority explicit
    possible_outcomes:
      - governance_candidate
      - reject_local_shortcut
      - ghost_promotion_record_missing
  authority_boundary:
    class: protected
    dan_required: true
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: true if repo/files mutate
    packet_type: mutation | code
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true for admitted docs/test/build jobs
    mode: dry_run | apply with approval
    target_lab: docs runtime
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - diff/proposal
      - review decision
  projection_target:
    - Source of Truth Map
    - Archive
    - Current State
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: true if promoted
    receipt_profile: minilab.governance.receipt_profile.v1
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - promotion-record-missing
      - parent-canon-conflict
      - governance-review-missing
```

### F2 — Promote Santo André Experiment to Doctrine

process_id: F2

runtime_dynamics:

    forbidden:
      - call intuition discovery
      - claim external recognition
      - promote doctrine

      - invariant present

      - doctrine_note_candidate

    class: protected for doctrine promotion
    dan_required: true
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: true if repo/docs mutation
    packet_type: mutation | publication
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true for admitted conformance/test/doc build
    mode: read_only | dry_run | apply with approval
    target_lab: research/docs runtime
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - experiment record
      - probe evidence
      - promotion decision

    - Santo André Experiment Registry
    - Source of Truth Map

    receipt_candidate_allowed: true

### F3 — Emit Errata

```yaml
process_id: F3
name: Emit errata
family: governance_change
status: future_formal
```

**Trigger**  
A non-normative error is discovered: typo, link, example, reference, wording that does not change MUST/SHOULD/MAY or semantics.

**Primary actor**  
Canon Librarian / Dan.

**Primary office**  
Canon Librarian.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Error is non-normative.
Affected document exists.
Errata path exists or is ghosted.
```

**Steps**

1. Classify as errata, not amendment.
2. Draft correction.
3. Record in errata log.
4. Apply correction if approved.
5. Preserve reference to original.

**Result**

```txt
Minor correction recorded without false version inflation.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
correction diff, errata log entry.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
normative change disguised as errata
old version not preserved
errata path missing
```

**Next process**

```txt
F1 if normative.
Archive if superseded.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Constitution
  jurisdiction: docs / archive
  supporting_offices:
    - Archive Keeper
    - Ghost Keeper
  operator_role: correct non-normative error transparently
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - identify typo/link/example issue
      - draft errata note
    forbidden:
      - hide normative change
      - rewrite source without record
  model_output_contract: Errata Note
  candidate_type: errata_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - non-normative classification
      - affected source named
      - errata record path
    possible_outcomes:
      - admissible_errata
      - route_to_F1
      - ghost_errata_log_missing
  authority_boundary:
    class: normal unless canon semantics affected
    dan_required: true if source is promoted canon
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: true if file mutation
    packet_type: mutation
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true for admitted doc patch/build
    mode: dry_run | apply with approval
    target_lab: docs runtime
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - diff
      - errata entry
  projection_target:
    - Archive
    - Source of Truth Map
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: false by default
    receipt_profile: none
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - errata-log-missing
      - normative-change-risk
```

---

### F4 — Retire Project or Repository

```yaml
process_id: F4
name: Retire Project or repository
family: governance_change
status: bootstrap_manual
```

**Trigger**  
A Project, repo, document set, app, process, or jurisdiction no longer belongs in active operation.

**Primary actor**  
Dan.

**Primary office**  
Archive Keeper / Canon Librarian.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Object exists.
Retirement reason is known.
Archive/supersession path exists or is ghosted.
```

**Steps**

1. Decide archive vs delete vs supersede.
2. Preserve history if needed.
3. Record retirement act.
4. Update registry/current state.
5. Ensure old material does not pretend to be current.

**Result**

```txt
Object is retired or archived cleanly.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
retirement act, archive location, registry/current state update.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
active material lost
archived material treated as current
retirement reason missing
```

**Next process**

```txt
B4 snapshot if significant.
Archive review.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Archive
  jurisdiction: Archive / Registry
  supporting_offices:
    - Canon Librarian
    - Ghost Keeper
  operator_role: preserve historical state while removing active status
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - summarize retirement reason
      - identify dependent refs
    forbidden:
      - delete without Dan
      - mark superseded without source
  model_output_contract: Archive Note / LogLineCandidate
  candidate_type: retirement_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - target identity stable
      - archive/supersession path explicit
      - reason stated
    possible_outcomes:
      - retire_candidate
      - supersede_candidate
      - ghost_archive_location_undecided
  authority_boundary:
    class: protected if deletion or jurisdiction removal
    dan_required: true
    execution_window_required: false unless automated destructive operation
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: true if repo/app/provider mutation
    packet_type: mutation
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true for admitted archive/export command
    mode: dry_run | apply with approval
    target_lab: docs/archive runtime
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - archive ref
      - registry update
      - retirement reason
  projection_target:
    - Archive
    - registry.entities
    - Current State
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: true for consequential retirement
    receipt_profile: minilab.retirement.receipt_profile.v1
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - archive-location-undecided
      - supersession-map-missing
      - retirement-reason-missing
```

---

## 9. Family G — Rhythms / Rites

Family G covers repeated institutional cadence.

---

### G1 — Morning Ritual

```yaml
process_id: G1
name: Morning ritual
family: rhythms
status: active_bootstrap
```

**Trigger**  
Start of day.

**Primary actor**  
Morning Scribe / Dan.

**Primary office**  
Morning Scribe.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Current State and Ghost Registry exist, or Day Zero template is used.
```

**Steps**

1. Read current state.
2. Read ghosts.
3. Check Casa, LAB, Pesquisa, Estado/Prova, Work/Requests, Needs Dan.
4. Name no more than five next acts unless Dan asks.
5. List promotion candidates.

**Result**

```txt
Minilab wakes honestly.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
Morning State report with evidence states.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
motivational briefing instead of state
missing proof hidden
stale state presented current
```

**Next process**

```txt
B1, B2, D1, Casa process, Research process, Authority packet.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Cockpit
  jurisdiction: Morning State
  supporting_offices:
    - LAB Reporter
    - Home Ops Planner
    - Research Registrar
    - Ghost Keeper
    - Authority Clerk
  operator_role: produce daily state handoff
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - summarize sources
      - cluster ghosts
      - suggest next acts
    forbidden:
      - invent state
      - mark verified without evidence
      - create projects
  model_output_contract: Morning State report
  candidate_type: daily_state_report
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - every section has evidence state
      - ghosts visible
      - Dan actions explicit
    possible_outcomes:
      - morning_state_admissible
      - ghost_current_state_missing
      - ghost_registry_missing
  authority_boundary:
    class: read_only
    dan_required: false for report; true for promotions/decisions
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: false unless next act becomes work packet
    packet_type: none
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: false unless delegated probe follows
    mode: none
    target_lab: none
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - source refs or source ghosts
  projection_target:
    - Morning State
    - Current State
    - Ghost Registry
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: false
    receipt_profile: none
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - morning-state-not-yet-run
      - current-state-missing
      - ghost-registry-missing
```

---

### G2 — Night Ritual

```yaml
process_id: G2
name: Night ritual
family: rhythms
status: optional_bootstrap
```

**Trigger**  
End of day.

**Primary actor**  
Dan / Morning Scribe equivalent.

**Primary office**  
Morning Scribe or Routing Clerk.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Day had meaningful activity or open ghosts.
```

**Steps**

1. Record what closed today.
2. Record what remains open.
3. Convert important unfinished items into ghosts or next acts.
4. Avoid fake closure.

**Result**

```txt
Day ends without losing open state.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
night note / closed day act / carried ghosts.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
forgotten open work
completion claimed without evidence
night ritual becomes guilt theater
```

**Next process**

```txt
G1 next morning.
B2 ghost review.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Cockpit
  jurisdiction: Daily Control Plane
  supporting_offices:
    - Ghost Keeper
  operator_role: preserve end-of-day state
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - summarize day
      - detect unresolved items
    forbidden:
      - claim completion without evidence
  model_output_contract: Night Handoff
  candidate_type: daily_closure_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - closed vs open distinguished
      - ghosts carried
      - evidence state declared
    possible_outcomes:
      - handoff_admissible
      - ghost_completion_unverified
  authority_boundary:
    class: read_only
    dan_required: false
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: false
    packet_type: none
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: false
    mode: none
    target_lab: none
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - handoff note
  projection_target:
    - Current State
    - Ghost Registry
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: false
    receipt_profile: none
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - end-of-day-handoff-missing
```

---

### G3 — Weekly Review

```yaml
process_id: G3
name: Weekly review
family: rhythms
status: bootstrap_manual
```

**Trigger**  
Weekly cadence, typically Friday.

**Primary actor**  
Dan / Morning Scribe / Ghost Keeper.

**Primary office**  
Ghost Keeper with Morning Scribe.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Current State and Ghost Registry exist or are ghosted.
```

**Steps**

1. Review open ghosts.
2. Review receipts/evidence if any.
3. Identify repeated gaps.
4. Decide what to promote, archive, or build.
5. Select next week focus.

**Result**

```txt
Week is digested into state, ghosts, and next acts.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
weekly review note, ghost actions, promotion candidates.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
review becomes narrative
old ghosts not carried
receipts overread
```

**Next process**

```txt
H2 if repeated gap needs process.
F1/F2 if promotion.
B4 if snapshot.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Cockpit
  jurisdiction: Weekly Review
  supporting_offices:
    - Ghost Keeper
    - Canon Librarian
    - Receipt Reviewer
  operator_role: convert week into decisions and ghosts
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - cluster recurring ghosts
      - summarize weekly changes
      - suggest promotions
    forbidden:
      - close ghosts without evidence
      - mark progress verified by narrative
  model_output_contract: Weekly Review report
  candidate_type: weekly_review_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - evidence states preserved
      - promotion candidates separated from promotions
      - ghosts carried
    possible_outcomes:
      - review_admissible
      - ghost_receipt_registry_missing
      - ghost_promotion_record_missing
  authority_boundary:
    class: read_only; protected for promotions
    dan_required: true for promotions/retirements
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: false unless work packets created
    packet_type: none
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: false unless review delegates verification
    mode: read_only
    target_lab: none
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - review note
  projection_target:
    - Current State
    - Ghost Registry
    - Work Request Ledger
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: false by default
    receipt_profile: none
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - weekly-review-missing
      - stale-ghosts-unreviewed
```

### G4 — Monthly Snapshot

```yaml
process_id: G4
name: Monthly snapshot
family: rhythms
status: future_formal
```

**Trigger**  
First day of month or before major changes.

**Primary actor**  
Archive Keeper / Registry.

**Primary office**  
Archive Keeper.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Snapshot source exists.
Storage path exists or ghost is carried.
```

**Steps**

1. Run B4 snapshot.
2. Store artifact.
3. Hash artifact.
4. Record snapshot act.
5. Update changelog or archive index.

**Result**

```txt
Monthly institutional snapshot exists.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
snapshot artifact and hash.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
storage undecided
snapshot missing hash
snapshot not indexed
```

**Next process**

```txt

Archive review.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Archive
  jurisdiction: Archive / Registry
  supporting_offices:
    - Canon Librarian
    - Ghost Keeper
  operator_role: preserve periodic state
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - summarize snapshot
      - identify changes since previous snapshot
    forbidden:
      - mutate snapshot
      - call snapshot receipt without receipt path
  model_output_contract: Snapshot Summary
  candidate_type: monthly_snapshot_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - source snapshot exists
      - hash status known
      - storage path known
    possible_outcomes:
      - snapshot_admissible
      - ghost_storage_undecided
      - ghost_hash_missing
  authority_boundary:
    class: normal
    dan_required: false unless storage policy changes
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: true if export/hash run by Hermes
    packet_type: verification
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true for admitted export/hash
    mode: read_only
    target_lab: registry runtime
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - artifact ref
      - hash
  projection_target:
    - Archive
    - Current State
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: true if formal snapshot receipt desired
    receipt_profile: minilab.snapshot.receipt_profile.v1
  ghost_path:

      - snapshot-hash-missing
```

### G5 — Quarterly Process Catalog Review

```yaml
process_id: G5
name: Quarterly process catalog review
family: rhythms
status: future_formal
```

**Trigger**  
Every quarter or after major architecture shift.

**Primary actor**  
Canon Librarian / Dan.

**Primary office**  
Canon Librarian.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Process Catalog exists.
Usage evidence or operator observation exists.
```

**Steps**

1. Review each process.
2. Mark used / unused / changed in practice / missing runtime dynamics.
3. Retire, amend, or add processes.
4. Version catalog.
5. Promote with Dan review.

**Result**

```txt
Catalog remains living, not fossilized.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
review notes, process changes, promotion decision.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
catalog drifts from practice
unused processes accumulate
missing processes remain implicit
```

**Next process**

```txt
H2 define new process.
F1 if doctrine changes.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Constitution
  jurisdiction: Process Catalog
  supporting_offices:
    - Routing Clerk
    - Ghost Keeper
  operator_role: keep process library aligned with lived operation
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - identify duplicate processes
      - suggest consolidation
      - detect missing runtime_dynamics
    forbidden:
      - delete process without review
      - promote amendments
  model_output_contract: Process Review Note
  candidate_type: catalog_review_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - every change classified
      - retirement/amendment source refs present
      - Dan promotion explicit
    possible_outcomes:
      - amendment_candidate
      - retirement_candidate
      - ghost_process_usage_unobserved
  authority_boundary:
    class: protected for promoted catalog change
    dan_required: true
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: true if file/repo mutation
    packet_type: mutation
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true for admitted docs build/check
    mode: dry_run | apply with approval
    target_lab: docs runtime
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - review note
      - diff if changed
  projection_target:
    - Source of Truth Map
    - Archive
    - Current State
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: true for promoted catalog version
    receipt_profile: minilab.process_catalog.receipt_profile.v1
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - process-catalog-runtime-dynamics-missing
      - process-usage-evidence-missing
```

## 10. Family H — Building New Processes

Family H defines how Minilab adds processes without improvising forever.

---

### H1 — Detect Missing Process

```yaml
process_id: H1
name: Detect missing process
family: process_creation
status: active_bootstrap
```

**Trigger**  
Dan or an operator catches repeated improvisation, uncertainty, or LLM being asked to decide how to do something.

**Primary actor**  
Any operator.

**Primary office**  
Routing Clerk.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Need does not fit existing process.
```

**Steps**

1. Stop or mark improvisation.
2. Record missing process statement.
3. If urgent, proceed as exception with ghost.
4. Route to H2 when repeated or important.

**Result**

```txt
Process gap becomes visible.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
missing process note, examples if available.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
improvisation becomes habit
LLM invents path
exception becomes hidden norm
```

**Next process**

```txt
H2 define new process.
E4 if LLM drift caused it.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Cockpit
  jurisdiction: Routing / Process Catalog
  supporting_offices:
    - Canon Librarian
    - Ghost Keeper
  operator_role: name process absence before it becomes drift
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - compare need to existing catalog
      - suggest closest process
    forbidden:
      - invent executable path
      - silently create process as canon
  model_output_contract: Process Gap Note
  candidate_type: process_gap_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - gap stated
      - urgency/exception marked
      - next owner named
    possible_outcomes:
      - open_process_gap
      - route_to_existing_process
      - exception_with_ghost
  authority_boundary:
    class: normal
    dan_required: true if process creation/promoted change
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: false unless urgent work packet created
    packet_type: none | executable
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: false unless urgent admitted work follows
    mode: none
    target_lab: none
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - process gap note
  projection_target:
    - Ghost Registry
    - Process Catalog backlog
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: false
    receipt_profile: none
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - process-missing
      - path-not-defined
```

---

### H2 — Define New Process

```yaml
process_id: H2
name: Define new process
family: process_creation
status: active_bootstrap
```

**Trigger**  
A process gap appears three times, blocks significant work, or requires stable operation.

**Primary actor**  
Canon Librarian / Dan.

**Primary office**  
Canon Librarian.

**Preconditions**

```txt
Process gap exists.
Examples or need are known.
Standard process shape is available.
```

**Steps**

1. Name process.
2. Choose family.
3. Fill standard process shape.
4. Add runtime_dynamics.
5. Identify ghosts.
6. Add as draft to catalog.
7. Promote only after Dan review.

**Result**

```txt
New process candidate exists.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
process draft, examples, promotion decision.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
process overfits one event
runtime dynamics omitted
process added without promotion
```

**Next process**

```txt
G5 catalog review.
F1 if doctrine affected.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Constitution
  jurisdiction: Process Catalog
  supporting_offices:
    - Routing Clerk
    - Ghost Keeper
  operator_role: formalize repeated practice into governed process
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - draft process template
      - identify runtime dynamics
      - find similar processes
    forbidden:
      - promote process
      - omit authority/ghost boundary
  model_output_contract: Process Draft
  candidate_type: process_definition_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - family selected
      - runtime_dynamics present
      - evidence/ghost paths present
      - promotion state candidate
    possible_outcomes:
      - process_candidate
      - reject_overfit_process
      - ghost_runtime_dynamics_missing
  authority_boundary:
    class: protected for catalog promotion
    dan_required: true
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: true if file/repo mutation
    packet_type: mutation
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: true for admitted docs check
    mode: dry_run | apply with approval
    target_lab: docs runtime
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - process draft
      - examples or reason
  projection_target:
    - Process Catalog
    - Source of Truth Map
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: true if promoted
    receipt_profile: minilab.process_catalog.receipt_profile.v1
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - process-examples-missing
      - runtime-dynamics-missing
      - promotion-record-missing
```

---

### H3 — Promote Recurring Improvisation to Process

```yaml
process_id: H3
name: Promote recurring improvisation to process
family: process_creation
status: active_bootstrap
```

**Trigger**  
Dan has done the same uncatalogued thing repeatedly.

**Primary actor**  
Routing Clerk / Canon Librarian.

**Primary office**  
Routing Clerk.

**Preconditions**

```txt
At least three occurrences exist, or one occurrence is critical enough.
```

**Steps**

1. Collect examples.
2. Extract common pattern.
3. Route to H2.
4. Archive or reference the improvisations.

**Result**

```txt
Recurring behavior becomes process candidate.
```

**Expected evidence**

```txt
examples, extracted pattern, H2 draft.
```

**Failure modes**

```txt
pattern misread
process overcomplicates simple habit
examples lost
```

**Next process**

```txt
H2 define new process.
```

**runtime_dynamics**

```yaml
runtime_dynamics:
  organ: Cockpit
  jurisdiction: Process Catalog backlog
  supporting_offices:
    - Canon Librarian
    - Ghost Keeper
  operator_role: detect repeated practice and route to formal process
  mini_llm_use:
    allowed:
      - cluster examples
      - suggest common steps
    forbidden:
      - declare process current
      - erase exceptions
  model_output_contract: Pattern Extraction Note
  candidate_type: recurring_process_candidate
  constitutional_runtime_boundary:
    checks:
      - recurrence evidence present
      - pattern scope explicit
      - H2 route declared
    possible_outcomes:
      - route_to_H2
      - ghost_examples_missing
      - reject_not_recurring
  authority_boundary:
    class: normal
    dan_required: true for promotion
    execution_window_required: false
  dispatch_boundary:
    required: false
    packet_type: none
  hermes_boundary:
    allowed: false
    mode: none
    target_lab: none
  evidence_return:
    required:
      - example refs
      - extracted pattern
  projection_target:
    - Process Catalog backlog
    - Ghost Registry if gap blocks work
  closure_path:
    receipt_candidate_allowed: false
    receipt_profile: none
  ghost_path:
    if_missing:
      - recurring-examples-missing
      - process-gap-unresolved
```

---

## 11. Initial Exposed Gaps

This catalog exposes known gaps rather than hiding them.

```txt
D5 — Machine heartbeat does not exist yet.
Hermes runtime not implemented.
Worker bridge absent.
Hash computation / JCS tooling may be missing.
audit.v_mobile_today may be planned, not observed.
Inbox storage is not fully decided.
Process runtime_dynamics must be reviewed after first operating week.
```

These are not failures.  
They are ghosts and build targets.

---

## 12. Relationship to 09 and 10

This catalog names processes.

```txt
09 — Vertical Runtime Doctrine
```

defines how each process moves through offices, operators, mini-LLMs, Constitutional Runtime, Authority, evidence, receipts, ghosts, and projections.

```txt
10 — Hermes Dispatch and Execution Contract
```

defines how admitted executable work becomes Hermes workorder and returns evidence.

Therefore:

```txt
08 says what process exists.
09 says how process happens.
10 says how process touches machines.
```

---

## 13. Acceptance Criteria

This catalog is accepted when:

```txt
1. Dan promotes or amends it.
2. Every process has a runtime_dynamics block.
3. Missing processes are listed as ghosts.
4. The catalog references 09 Vertical Runtime Doctrine.
5. The catalog references 10 Hermes Dispatch and Execution Contract.
6. First operating week uses at least Morning State, Inbox triage, LAB health, and Ghost review.
7. After use, G5 review updates the catalog from lived evidence.
```

---

## 14. Final Formulation

```txt
A process is not a checklist.
A process is a remembered path through the institution.

It begins with a trigger.
It names an office.
It declares its sources.
It permits or forbids mini-LLM assistance.
It produces candidates, dispatch, evidence, receipts, ghosts, or projections.
It does not let motion become truth.
```

Portuguese:

```txt
Um processo não é checklist.
Um processo é um caminho lembrado pela instituição.

Ele começa com um gatilho.
Ele nomeia um cargo.
Ele declara suas fontes.
Ele permite ou proíbe auxílio de mini-LLM.
Ele produz candidatos, dispatch, evidência, receipts, ghosts ou projeções.
Ele não deixa movimento virar verdade.
```

Convertido - criei o **08 - Minilab Process Catalog** como versão canon candidate, já no desenho novo.

Ele preserva o catálogo que você mandou, mas agora em forma de biblioteca:

```txt id="wb5g4t"
A - Individual Acts / Writing the World
B - Reading and State
C - Information Intake
D - LAB / Workers / Hermes
E - Work with LLMs
F - Governance and Change
G - Rhythms / Rites
H - Building New Processes
```

E cada processo ganhou o bloco `runtime_dynamics`, conectando com:

```txt id="n0qetr"
office
operator_role
mini_llm_use
Constitutional Runtime
Authority
Dispatch
Hermes
evidence_return
projection_target
closure_path
ghost_path
```
