**document: **

# minilab.work Frontend - Control Plane + Santo André Laboratory

**Status:** versão final de desenho técnico e produto  
**Camada:** frontend / cockpit / superfície operacional  
**Instância:** Santo André Laboratory  
**Domínio:** minilab.work  
**Parent concepts:** LogLine Foundation, LogLine Lab, Santo André Laboratory, minilab.work  
**Regra-mãe:** o frontend opera uma instância concreta de LogLine Lab; ele não redefine o conceito público de LogLine Lab.

---

## 0. Decisão central

`minilab.work` é o frontend, cockpit e presença digital de uma instância concreta de LogLine Lab: **Santo André Laboratory**.

Ele também é o control plane pessoal do Dan Voulez para operar a infraestrutura que sustenta essa instância:

```txt
computadores
LABs
runtimes
Hermes
agentes
operadores
tokens
credenciais
workorders
evidências
ghosts
receipts
relatórios
publicações
estado operacional
```

O frontend **não é** o LogLine Lab público.

O frontend **não é** a LogLine Foundation.

O frontend **não é** o canon.

O frontend **não é** o runtime.

O frontend **não é** fonte semântica de verdade.

Forma curta:

```txt
LogLine Foundation é a gramática.
LogLine Lab é o kit/prática pública.
CLI/labd é o núcleo operacional desacoplado.
Santo André Laboratory é a primeira instância concreta.
minilab.work é o cockpit dessa instância.
```

Forma operacional:

```txt
LogLine Lab public kit = primitives + manifest + CLI/labd + runtime discipline.
Santo André Laboratory = living LogLine Lab instance.
minilab.work = pitwall, frontend, digital presence and personal control plane.
```

---

## 1. Separação institucional

### 1.1 LogLine Foundation

Responsável por:

```txt
canon simples
gramática
ato de 9 slots
semântica fundacional
conformance
hash discipline
receipt discipline
governance upstream
```

Não é:

```txt
dashboard
app
cockpit
infraestrutura pessoal
Santo André
minilab.work
```

A Foundation define a gramática que pode ser carregada.

---

### 1.2 LogLine Developer Community

Responsável por:

```txt
implementações
SDKs
adapters
exemplos
pacotes
conformance tooling
instaladores
distribuição
integrações
documentação para builders
```

A comunidade constrói ao redor da Foundation.

Ela não governa a infraestrutura privada do Dan.

---

### 1.3 LogLine Lab

Responsável por fornecer o kit público para criar laboratórios LogLine.

Inclui, conceitualmente:

```txt
CLI
labd
manifest
act store
runtime registry
ghost registry
probe runner
evidence registry
receipt preparation
report generator
lab clock
project canon
mandatory hooks
projectors
standards adapters
local overlays
```

O LogLine Lab deve funcionar sem `minilab.work`.

O núcleo operacional deve existir fora de qualquer frontend.

Forma curta:

```txt
LogLine Lab é o kit e a prática.
CLI/labd é o seu núcleo operacional.
```

Não dizer:

```txt
LogLine Lab é a CLI.
```

Dizer:

```txt
O core operacional do LogLine Lab é CLI/labd/runtime.
```

---

### 1.4 Santo André Laboratory

Santo André Laboratory é a primeira instância concreta de LogLine Lab.

É uma instituição viva para estudar LogLine em movimento:

```txt
acts
engines
runtimes
projectors
ghosts
receipts
intervals
hooks
experiment loops
AI-to-act translation
operator behavior
evidence discipline
promotion control
what runs natively above software
```

Santo André Laboratory não é só uma seção do frontend.

É o Lab.

`minilab.work` é a superfície pela qual esse Lab aparece, opera e se deixa ver.

---

### 1.5 minilab.work

`minilab.work` é:

```txt
frontend
cockpit
pitwall
digital presence
control plane pessoal
superfície humana
janela operacional
```

Ele integra:

```txt
Dan
Santo André Laboratory
LogLine Lab CLI/labd
Hermes
LABs
máquinas
runtimes
agents
workorders
ghosts
evidências
receipts
relatórios
publicações
infraestrutura pessoal
```

Ele não é:

```txt
Foundation
Lab público genérico
canon
runtime soberano
database semântico
executor final
```

---

## 2. Regra de desacoplamento

O frontend nunca é fonte de verdade.

O frontend pode:

```txt
visualizar
propor
rotear
chamar CLI
chamar labd
abrir workorders candidatos
mostrar ghosts
mostrar evidências
mostrar receipts
mostrar máquinas
mostrar hooks
mostrar intervalos
mostrar relatórios
mostrar estado operacional
preparar decisão para Dan
```

O frontend não pode:

```txt
alterar canon diretamente
fechar receipt sem evidência
executar comando protegido sem workorder admitido
tratar projeção como verdade
inventar evidência
apagar ghost silenciosamente
escrever estado sem ato correspondente
transformar chat em execução
transformar UI card em autoridade
```

Forma curta:

```txt
Frontend projects.
CLI/labd operates.
Hermes executes admitted work.
LogLine Acts carry meaning.
Evidence supports.
Receipts close scope.
Ghosts preserve absence.
```

---

## 3. Natureza do frontend

O frontend deve parecer menos “chat com IA” e mais **pitwall de laboratório**.

Metáfora central:

```txt
Pitwall is not chat with a terminal.
Pitwall is a shared operational surface with radio.
```

O humano e o Translator olham para o mesmo objeto operacional.

A conversa é rádio.

A superfície é estado.

O trabalho real está em:

```txt
terminal
TUI
act graph
current interval
hooks
lanes
evidence strip
ghost board
runtime state
machine state
diffs
tests
receipts
reports
```

O LLM não deve ficar “olhando para o humano”.

Ele deve olhar para o mesmo trabalho que o humano e narrar o que vê.

Forma curta:

```txt
Human and Translator face the same machine.
The human steers.
The Translator structures.
The Operator executes.
The Runtime observes.
LogLine carries state.
```

---

## 4. Lei do frontend

```txt
The frontend may display.
The frontend may request.
The frontend may route.
The frontend may prepare.
The frontend may call CLI/labd APIs.

The frontend may not govern canon.
The frontend may not execute protected consequence.
The frontend may not treat projection as truth.
The frontend may not close receipts.
The frontend may not invent evidence.
The frontend may not erase ghosts.
```

O frontend é superfície.

A semântica vem de LogLine Acts.

A operação vem de CLI/labd/Hermes/runtimes admitidos.

A consequência vem de gates, authority, workorders e evidência.

---

## 5. Produto

Nome do produto/site:

```txt
minilab.work
```

Instância operada:

```txt
Santo André Laboratory
```

Descrição curta:

```txt
Frontend and operational cockpit for Santo André Laboratory.
```

Descrição pública:

```txt
minilab.work is the digital pitwall of Santo André Laboratory:
a LogLine Lab instance for studying LogLine in motion,
operating with acts, runtimes, evidence, ghosts, receipts and reports.
```

Descrição interna:

```txt
minilab.work is Dan’s personal control plane for operating Santo André Laboratory
and the infrastructure that sustains it.
```

---

## 6. Princípio de interface

O frontend deve preservar uma estrutura de três planos.

### Plane 1 - Lab / Authority / Navigation

Mostra:

```txt
lab identity
active jurisdiction
active mode
navigation
authority state
current operator lane
Dan-required decisions
```

### Plane 2 - Machine Surface

Superfície principal.

Pode mostrar:

```txt
terminal
TUI
diff viewer
test runner
runtime output
machine status
lab timeline
current workbench
experiment loop
code lab
```

É a pista.

O chat não é o centro.

### Plane 3 - Radio / Inspector / Evidence

Mostra:

```txt
Translator narration
context
trace
relations
JSON
runtime envelope
evidence refs
ghosts
receipts
next safe act
```

O radio não substitui o estado.

Ele interpreta e estrutura a visão compartilhada.

---

## 7. Top Bar - Lab / Interval / Canon

A top bar deve mostrar o contexto operacional mínimo:

```txt
active lab
active interval
active experiment
Foundation canon version
Lab profile version
Project canon version
canon hash
active branch
active lane
clock status
```

Exemplo:

```txt
Santo André Laboratory
Interval: exp-001 / constructive-release-semantics
Lane: Operator
Branch: if_ok
Foundation: logline.foundation@1.0.0
Lab Profile: logline-lab.practice@0.1.0
Project Canon: project-canon@0.13.0 / sha256:...
Clock: active
```

Regra:

```txt
Foundation Canon ≠ Lab Profile ≠ Project Canon ≠ Local Overlay.
```

A UI deve deixar essa separação visível.

---

## 8. Tela inicial - Daily Lab State

Ao abrir `minilab.work`, a sensação deve ser:

```txt
I installed a lab instrument.
It knows its state.
It knows what is unresolved.
It does not pretend.
```

A tela inicial deve ser um **Daily Lab State**, não um dashboard genérico.

Exemplo:

```txt
Santo André Laboratory is running.

Clock: active
Foundation: logline.foundation@1.0.0
Lab Profile: logline-lab.practice@0.1.0
Project Canon: project-canon@0.13.0
Open ghosts: 7
Receipt candidates: 2
Stale probes: 1
Mandatory hook failures: 0
Machines online: 3 / 4
Last evidence captured: 12 minutes ago

Next safe act:
  review ghost: test_failure_after_operator_edit
```

O Daily Lab State deve responder:

```txt
what is known now?
what is unknown?
what is declared?
what has evidence?
what remains ghost?
what needs Dan?
what is the next smallest honest act?
```

---

## 9. Left Rail - Act Graph / Ghosts / Receipts

Abas mínimas:

```txt
Acts
Ghosts
Receipts
Experiments
Runtimes
Hooks
Canon
Reports
```

Deve mostrar:

```txt
parent act
current act
candidate acts
open ghosts
receipt candidates
blocked closures
active experiment
active interval
runtime state
```

A Left Rail não é menu decorativo.

Ela é o mapa de estado institucional.

---

## 10. Center - Machine Surface

O centro é a superfície onde o trabalho real aparece.

Modos possíveis:

```txt
Lab State
Code Lab
Operator Console
Terminal / TUI
Experiment Loop
Runtime Output
Diff Viewer
Test Runner
Report Builder
Project Canon
Ghost Board
Receipt Review
```

Regra:

```txt
The shared surface is state.
The radio is coordination.
```

O centro não deve ser um chat dominante.

---

## 11. Right Rail - Race Radio / Translator

O Translator aparece como rádio, legenda operacional e estruturação.

Formato preferido:

```txt
I see...
I do not see...
This act claims...
This evidence supports...
This ghost remains...
The next safe act is...
```

Evitar:

```txt
I did...
I verified...
It is done...
Trust me...
Production ready...
```

Sem evidência, o Translator não fala como fato.

O Translator deve ser treinado visualmente a apontar para objetos da superfície:

```txt
act
ghost
evidence item
hook
receipt candidate
runtime output
workorder
canon delta
```

Ele deve manter estado epistêmico, não conversa infinita.

Frase-guia:

```txt
The Translator does not keep a conversation alive.
The Translator keeps epistemic state alive.
```

---

## 12. Bottom Strip - Evidence / Hooks / Gates

Sempre visível quando houver operação.

Mostra:

```txt
mandatory hooks applied
hooks pending
tests running
exit codes
stdout hash
stderr hash
diff hash
artifact hashes
runtime envelope
blocked gates
execution window
next required evidence
secret redaction status
```

A bottom strip é a faixa de realidade.

Regra:

```txt
Evidence is reality contact.
Receipt is scoped closure.
```

---

## 13. Lanes operacionais

Forge, Translator, Operator, Evidence Lane e Receipt Review são **lanes operacionais**, não órgãos fundadores.

Eles operam sob órgãos existentes:

```txt
Cockpit
Santo André Laboratory
Authority
LAB
Evidence / Receipts / Ghosts
Registry / Estado
```

Lanes mínimas:

```txt
Forge
Translator
Operator
Evidence
Receipt Review
Report
```

---

## 14. Forge Lane

Entrada:

```txt
messy prompt
bad prompt
domain-specialized input
unclear human intention
foreign-language input
logs broken beyond immediate translation
legal/contractual input
research idea
```

Função:

```txt
melhorar prompt
rotear para contexto especialista
traduzir linguagem difícil
clarificar intenção
reduzir ruído antes do Translator
```

Saída:

```txt
normalized prompt
detected intent
assumptions
ambiguities
recommended next lane
```

Forge pode usar LLM fresco ou especialista.

Forge não executa.

Forge não fecha.

Forge não promove.

Botão de UI:

```txt
✨ Magic Prompt / Route Prompt
```

Regra:

```txt
Do not send bad prompts directly to Translator.
```

---

## 15. Translator Lane

Entrada:

```txt
normalized prompt
known context refs
current branch
open ghosts
current project canon
current interval
```

Função:

```txt
intenção clara → candidate acts
```

O Translator:

```txt
extrai atos
nomeia ghosts
detecta slots ausentes
propõe branches
propõe workorders
pergunta só o mínimo bloqueante
```

Ele não executa terminal.

Ele não chama Hermes diretamente.

Ele não fecha receipt.

Ele pode dizer:

```txt
Este prompt ainda não é traduzível.
Envie para Forge/Magic Prompt primeiro.
```

Saída:

```txt
candidate LogLine Act
ghost candidates
minimal question
workorder candidate
routing note
```

---

## 16. Operator Lane

O Operator opera uma máquina.

Não opera uma bola de cristal.

Entrada:

```txt
admitted workorder
allowed actions
forbidden actions
machine state
declared hooks
evidence requirements
runtime boundary
```

Saída:

```txt
runtime observation
command transcript
diff
test result
failure ghost
evidence candidate
```

Se faltar algo:

```txt
if_doubt
ghost
clarification request
reject workorder
```

Princípio:

```txt
Operators operate machines, not crystal balls.
```

---

## 17. Runtime

Runtime executa ou observa.

Pode ser:

```txt
terminal local
Hermes
LAB
CI
script
worker
MCP tool
human procedure
browser runtime
model runtime
database runtime
```

Runtime não é autoridade.

Runtime success não é receipt.

Runtime output pode virar evidência.

Runtime envelope deve preservar:

```txt
runtime_id
engine_id
run_id
started_at
finished_at
mode
status
hashes
secret_redacted
previous refs
```

---

## 18. Evidence Lane

Captura:

```txt
stdout
stderr
exit code
diff
test result
artifact hash
screenshot
sensor result
manual witness
runtime envelope
provider response
conformance output
```

Evidence Lane não fecha escopo.

Ela fornece material para Receipt Review.

Regra:

```txt
LLM claim is not evidence.
Runtime output may become evidence.
Receipt closes only scoped claim.
```

---

## 19. Receipt Review Lane

Entrada:

```txt
claim
evidence refs
ghosts
scope
receipt profile
canon version
runtime/conformance state
```

Saída:

```txt
receipt candidate
closed receipt
closure rejected
more evidence required
ghost preserved
```

Receipts devem separar:

```txt
receipt candidates
closed receipts
blocked receipts
rejected closures
```

Bloquear sempre:

```txt
runtime success = receipt
model output = evidence
confidence = proof
projection = truth
broad claim from narrow evidence
```

---

## 20. Report Lane

Relatórios são gerados a partir do Lab.

Eles não são romance.

Tipos:

```txt
daily report
weekly report
experiment report
ghost review
receipt review
misuse study
canon delta report
runtime autopsy
publication draft
```

Todo relatório deve incluir:

```txt
claims
evidence
ghosts
receipts
limits
next acts
promotion state
```

Um relatório pode preparar publicação.

Um relatório não é receipt por si mesmo.

---

## 21. Project Canon

O frontend deve ter tela de Project Canon.

Ela mostra:

```txt
canon version
canon hash
parent canon
mandatory hooks
experiment loops
lane definitions
variable schedules
quality gates
active overlays
pending canon deltas
rejected canon deltas
canon ghosts
```

Separação obrigatória:

```txt
Foundation Canon
Lab Practice/Profile
Lab Instance Canon
Project Canon
Local Overlay
```

O LLM pode sugerir mudanças de canon.

Sugestão não vira canon automaticamente.

Fluxo:

```txt
suggest canon delta
→ candidate act
→ canon quality gate
→ accepted/rejected/ghosted
→ new canon version
```

Telas mínimas:

```txt
Current Canon
Pending Deltas
Rejected Deltas
Canon Ghosts
```

---

## 22. Mandatory Hooks

Hooks não são UI hooks.

Hooks são intervenções científicas ou operacionais obrigatórias definidas por:

```txt
project canon
lab profile
experiment loop
authority policy
```

O frontend mostra hooks.

`labd` ou CLI deve aplicar/enforce hooks.

Runtime reporta evidência de hook.

Receipt Review bloqueia closure se hook obrigatório estiver ausente.

Exemplo:

```yaml
hook_id: after_operator_edit.run_verification_plan.v1
trigger: after_lane.operator_edit
mandatory: true

verification_plan:
  commands:
    - cargo test --workspace

capture:
  - stdout
  - stderr
  - exit_code
  - diff_hash

on_pass:
  lane: evidence
  did: capture_test_evidence

on_fail:
  lane: if_doubt
  did: open_test_failure_ghost
```

Regra:

```txt
The project remembers the method.
The model only plays its lane.
```

Se hook obrigatório não rodou:

```txt
turn invalid
open hook_missing ghost
block receipt closure
```

---

## 23. Experiment Loop

Todo experimento deve repetir um loop registrado.

Loop padrão:

```txt
Forge
→ Translator
→ Operator
→ Evidence
→ Receipt Review
→ Report
```

Cada turn carrega:

```txt
turn_id
experiment_id
canon_version
canon_hash
lane
branch
mandatory hooks
variables
required outputs
forbidden actions
```

O frontend deve mostrar esse contrato antes da execução.

Exemplo visual:

```txt
This turn belongs to:
  experiment: exp-001
  loop: default_experiment_loop.v1
  lane: operator
  canon: project-canon@0.13.0
  mandatory after-hook: run_verification_plan.v1
```

---

## 24. Intervals

O frontend deve representar intervalos LogLine.

Um intervalo é um campo de atos entre:

```txt
start boundary act
finish boundary act
```

Dentro dele podem existir:

```txt
candidate acts
simulation paths
real runtime runs
observations
evidence
ghosts
receipts
projections
reports
next acts
```

A UI deve mostrar:

```txt
interval start
current branch
branch status
real runs
simulated paths
runtime observations
result acts
finish criteria
open ghosts
```

Regra:

```txt
A result act is not an ending.
It may become input to the next interval.
```

---

## 25. Code Lab

Code Lab é parte do frontend.

Mas não é playground.

É um governed workbench.

Deve comunicar:

```txt
candidate artifacts
controlled code work
protected command boundaries
evidence capture
logs
files
benchmarks
review
no mutation without gate
```

Code Lab deve separar:

```txt
code draft
patch candidate
verification run
runtime output
evidence item
receipt candidate
ghost
```

Regra:

```txt
Generated code is artifact.
Verified behavior requires runtime evidence.
Operational consequence requires promotion control.
```

Visualmente:

```txt
work chat cards are dark
file list is dark
preview surface is dark or explicitly external
logs/evidence strip is dark
tabs are dark
badges use semantic states
selected states use blue accent/border
code/file surfaces are dark and monospace
```

Nunca parecer:

```txt
generic coding playground
generic AI IDE
chatbot that edits magically
```

Deve parecer:

```txt
controlled lab workbench
```

---

## 26. Operator Console

Operator Console mostra máquinas e ações permitidas.

Nunca deve parecer “chatbot executando mágica”.

Mostra:

```txt
machine
repo
cwd
runtime
workorder
allowed actions
forbidden actions
commands planned
commands run
current process
last output
diff
test state
evidence required
secret policy
execution window
```

Se faltar clareza:

```txt
ask Translator
open ghost
reject workorder
```

---

## 27. Ghost Board

Ghosts são superfície de primeira classe.

Cada ghost mostra:

```txt
what is missing
why it matters
what it blocks
owner / next act
how it could be closed or narrowed
source act
opened_at
age
status
```

Tipos importantes:

```txt
prompt_too_ambiguous
workorder_underconstrained
missing_evidence_path
hook_missing
canon_invalid
test_failure_after_edit
projection_drift
claimed_action_without_observation
receipt_overclosure_risk
source_refs_missing
runtime_receipts_missing
publication_receipts_missing
mcp_host_runtime_observation_missing
```

Ghost não é fracasso.

Ghost é ausência preservada.

Frase:

```txt
A ghost is the system refusing to lie.
```

---

## 28. Evidence Strip

Sempre visível quando houver execução.

Mostra:

```txt
stdout hash
stderr hash
exit code
diff hash
artifact refs
runtime envelope
observed_at
redaction status
scope
limits
evidence state
```

Estados possíveis:

```txt
unknown
planned
declared
observed
evidence_captured
verified
ghost
retired
superseded
```

A Evidence Strip deve impedir que a UI pareça confiante sem prova.

---

## 29. Receipts

Tela de receipts deve separar:

```txt
receipt candidates
closed receipts
blocked receipts
rejected closures
```

Para cada receipt:

```txt
claim closed
evidence refs
scope closed
scope not closed
ghosts remaining
runtime/reviewer
hashes
canon version
conformance state
```

Regra:

```txt
Receipt closes only declared scope.
```

A UI deve bloquear linguagem como:

```txt
system works
production ready
all regressions absent
future behavior guaranteed
```

salvo se o receipt tiver escopo explícito que suporte exatamente isso.

---

## 30. Promotion Control

O frontend deve tratar promoção para estado confiável como problema central.

A distinção principal não é:

```txt
good model
vs
bad model
```

É:

```txt
generated artifact
vs
trusted operational consequence
```

Promotion control deve acompanhar quatro eixos:

```txt
artifact_state
evidence_state
trust_state
visibility_state
```

### artifact_state

```txt
generated
drafted
staged
admitted
rejected
```

### evidence_state

```txt
none
claimed
observed
source-backed
runtime-backed
receipt-backed
ghost
```

### trust_state

```txt
untrusted
reviewable
provisionally-trusted
trusted-for-scope
trusted-operational-consequence
```

### visibility_state

```txt
private
internal
publication-candidate
public
deprecated
retracted
```

Regra:

```txt
Public does not mean receipt-backed.
Runtime-backed does not mean safe.
Source-backed requires source refs.
Receipt-backed requires receipt refs.
```

Forma forte:

```txt
The critical infrastructure problem is no longer generating artifacts.
It is controlling how artifacts become trusted operational consequence.
```

---

## 31. Claim Ledger

O frontend deve visualizar um claim ledger.

Shape conceitual:

```json
{
  "claim_id": "",
  "artifact_ref": "",
  "claim_text": "",
  "claim_class": "",
  "artifact_state": "",
  "evidence_state": "",
  "trust_state": "",
  "visibility_state": "",
  "source_refs": [],
  "runtime_refs": [],
  "receipt_refs": [],
  "ghost_refs": [],
  "verification_gates": [],
  "authority_level": "",
  "promotion_blockers": [],
  "allowed_next_states": [],
  "last_reviewed_at": "",
  "last_verified_at": "",
  "published_at": "",
  "deprecated_at": "",
  "retracted_at": ""
}
```

O campo `allowed_next_states` é obrigatório para promotion control real.

Proibir saltos como:

```txt
generated → trusted-operational-consequence
source-claimed → receipt-backed
runtime-success → system-trusted
public → receipt-backed without receipt_refs
```

---

## 32. Reports

Relatórios devem nascer de estado, não de improviso.

Tipos mínimos:

```txt
Daily Lab Expedition
Daily Lab State
Weekly Lab Report
Experiment Report
Ghost Review
Receipt Review
Misuse Study
Canon Delta Report
Runtime Autopsy
Publication Draft
```

Todo relatório deve incluir:

```txt
claims
evidence refs
ghosts
receipt refs
limits
promotion state
next acts
```

Publicações devem respeitar:

```txt
citations for external claims
evidence labels for internal claims
hypothesis markers for speculation
publication receipt after posting
```

---

## 33. Control Plane pessoal

Essa parte pertence a `minilab.work`, não ao LogLine Lab público.

Módulos possíveis:

```txt
Computers
LABs
Runtimes
Hermes
Agents
Tokens / Credentials
Backups
Queues
Jobs
Cost / Usage
Network / Tunnels
Deployments
Storage
Personal automations
```

Tudo que for consequencial deve se conectar ao Lab por:

```txt
acts
workorders
authority
execution windows
evidence
receipts
ghosts
```

Exemplo:

```txt
minilab.work sees Mac mini is down
→ emits observation candidate
→ if relevant, opens ghost in Santo André
→ if authorized, prepares workorder
→ Operator/Hermes executes
→ evidence captured
→ receipt/ghost updated
```

---

## 34. Comunicação com CLI/labd

O frontend deve preferir chamar APIs/CLI estáveis.

Exemplos:

```bash
logline-lab status
logline-lab doctor
logline-lab canon status
logline-lab act emit
logline-lab ghost list
logline-lab probe run
logline-lab evidence add
logline-lab receipt prepare
logline-lab report generate
```

Ou via `labd`:

```txt
local API
IPC
WebSocket events
read-only projections
explicit workorder endpoints
event stream
```

O frontend não deve depender de banco interno como fonte primária.

O banco pode servir projeções.

A semântica vem do act graph.

---

## 35. Hermes / Workorders

O frontend deve visualizar o contrato Hermes.

Caminho correto:

```txt
intent
→ process
→ dispatch packet
→ runtime admission
→ authority classification
→ Hermes workorder
→ LAB execution
→ evidence packet
→ receipt / ghost / projection
```

Caminho proibido:

```txt
chat message
→ Hermes command
→ claimed completion
```

Hermes recebe workorders.

Não recebe desejos.

Hermes executa.

Não governa.

Hermes retorna evidência.

Não fecha receipt.

---

## 36. Segurança e secrets

Regras absolutas:

```txt
No secret values in browser payloads.
No secret values in logs.
No secret values in workorders.
No secret values in receipts.
No env dump.
Service role server-only.
Secret names may appear when allowed.
Secret values must never appear.
```

Se redaction não puder ser garantido:

```txt
ghost: secret-redaction-unverified
```

Frontend deve mostrar:

```txt
redaction status
secret policy
credential scope
runtime boundary
```

---

## 37. Autenticação e autoridade

Auth do frontend não é autoridade institucional por si só.

Login prova sessão.

Não prova permissão ampla.

A UI deve distinguir:

```txt
credential
passport
visa
workorder
execution window
receipt
```

Forma curta:

```txt
Credential proves bearer.
Passport proves institutional identity.
Visa proves scoped permission.
Workorder proves admitted execution.
Receipt proves scoped closure.
```

---

## 38. Design visual

O frontend é dark-mode nativo.

Linguagem visual:

```txt
matte black / near-black background
charcoal panels
subtle borders
blue primary action
restrained green for valid/healthy
amber/yellow for ghost/warning
red only for destructive/rejected
compact technical typography
dense but breathable layout
```

Evitar:

```txt
bright white panels
generic SaaS dashboard
pastel AI app styling
generic purple chatbot branding
consumer admin panel
```

A sensação deve ser:

```txt
laboratory cockpit
command tower
pitwall
controlled workbench
instrument panel
```

Não:

```txt
chat app
IDE clone
marketing dashboard
```

---

## 39. Dark-mode CSS tokens

Tokens recomendados:

```txt
--background
--foreground
--panel
--panel-muted
--card
--border
--muted
--muted-foreground
--primary
--primary-foreground
--success
--warning
--destructive
--ghost
```

Auditar vazamentos light-mode:

```txt
bg-white
text-black
text-gray-900
border-gray-200
bg-slate-50
bg-neutral-50
default white inputs
default white dialogs
default white popovers
unstyled white code blocks
```

---

## 40. Instalação e produto

O LogLine Lab público deve ter:

```txt
CLI install
packages
updates
doctor
version
portable mode
```

`minilab.work` pode ter:

```txt
web app
desktop app
private auth
personal control plane
Santo André integration
public/private surfaces
```

O frontend é substituível.

O Lab deve continuar funcionando sem ele.

---

## 41. Relação com Pitwall

Pitwall inspira:

```txt
embedded terminal
race radio
mission panel
fleet lanes
timeline
diff panel
claims/evidence tracking
visual gates
repo watcher
git monitor
command detector
test detector
local event ledger
```

Mas a versão LogLine troca “MVP cockpit internals” por:

```txt
LogLine Acts
runtime envelopes
mandatory hooks
project canon
ghost registry
evidence registry
receipt discipline
content addressing
lab CLI/labd as source of operation
```

Pitwall é padrão de interface.

LogLine é protocolo.

Santo André é o Lab.

minilab.work é a superfície.

---

## 42. Frases de produto

```txt
Natural language is steering.
The shared surface is state.
LogLine is coordination.
Evidence is reality.
```

```txt
The project remembers the method.
The model only plays its lane.
```

```txt
Operators operate machines, not crystal balls.
```

```txt
The Translator does not keep a conversation alive.
The Translator keeps epistemic state alive.
```

```txt
Let humans speak richly.
Let Operators receive narrowly.
Let runtimes answer evidentially.
Let receipts close sparsely.
```

```txt
A Lab without a clock is a folder with ambition.
```

```txt
Generation is no longer scarce.
Trust is.
```

---

## 43. Acceptance Criteria

A versão inicial de `minilab.work` é aceitável se ela demonstrar:

```txt
1. Santo André Laboratory aparece como Lab principal.
2. minilab.work aparece como frontend/cockpit, não como Foundation.
3. Daily Lab State existe.
4. Ghosts são visíveis como primeira classe.
5. Evidence Strip aparece quando houver execução.
6. Receipts são separados de evidence e runtime success.
7. Code Lab é governed workbench, não playground.
8. Operator Console mostra máquina, workorder, allowed/forbidden actions e evidence required.
9. Project Canon mostra hooks, version, hash, deltas e ghosts.
10. Frontend não fecha receipt sozinho.
11. Frontend não executa protected action sem gate/workorder.
12. Dark mode é nativo.
13. CLI/labd boundary está explícito.
14. Hermes recebe workorders, não chat.
15. Promotion control está representado por estados separados.
```

---

## 44. Open Ghosts

```txt
labd-interface-unimplemented
logline-lab-cli-contract-unfinalized
project-canon-schema-unpromoted
mandatory-hooks-enforcement-unimplemented
daily-lab-state-projection-unimplemented
ghost-board-data-source-unconfirmed
evidence-strip-runtime-integration-missing
receipt-review-lane-unimplemented
operator-console-workorder-integration-missing
hermes-runtime-not-integrated
claim-ledger-schema-unpromoted
promotion-control-state-machine-unimplemented
frontend-auth-to-passport-visa-binding-missing
secret-redaction-unverified
dark-mode-code-lab-incomplete
santo-andre-public-private-boundary-unsettled
```

---

## 45. Definição final

O frontend de `minilab.work` é o cockpit privado e a presença digital de **Santo André Laboratory**, a primeira instância concreta de um LogLine Lab.

Ele monta uma superfície humana sobre:

```txt
LogLine Lab CLI
labd
Santo André practice
computadores
LABs
runtimes
agents
Hermes
workorders
evidence
ghosts
receipts
reports
Dan’s personal infrastructure
```

Sua missão é permitir que humano, Translator, Operator e Runtime olhem para o mesmo trabalho, sem misturar suas funções.

Forma final:

```txt
LogLine Foundation is the grammar.
LogLine Lab is the public kit and practice.
CLI/labd is the operational core.
Santo André Laboratory is the first living instance.
minilab.work is the pitwall.
Hermes is the hand.
LogLine is the wire.
Evidence returns.
Ghosts stay visible.
Receipts close narrowly.
Dan signs consequence.
```

---

## 46. Signature

```txt
We Trust and Build with LogLine.
```

>
> **Especificação delta sem referências diretas**
>
> O usuário pede uma especificação delta, então provavelmente não preciso incluir citações diretas dentro do documento. No entanto, posso mencionar que a base é "baseado no contrato Hermes". Não é necessário um arquivo de pesquisa profundo, e posso usar fragmentos de fontes para as citações, mesmo que faltem números de linhas.
>
> Pensado para 12s

Perfeito. O delta aqui não é “refazer UI”. É **traduzir a UI atual para a identidade final**: `minilab.work` como pitwall do **Santo André Laboratory**, mantendo o que já funciona e corrigindo a semântica. Base: Process Catalog, Vertical Runtime, Hermes Contract, Current State, Source of Truth Map, Organs/Jurisdictions, Practice Profile e Santo André Modus Operandi. `08 — Minilab Process Catalog.md` `09_vertical_runtime_doctrine.md` `10_hermes_dispatch_and_execution_contract.md` `06_current_state_v_0.md` `03_source_of_truth_map.md` `02_organs_and_jurisdictions.md` `12_minilab_logline_practice_profile_decisions.md` `11_santo-andre-lab-modus-operandi-doc-11-confirmed-by-witness-patch-v2.md`

**document: **

# minilab.work Frontend - Spec de Implementação do Delta UI

**Status:** implementação orientada / delta spec  
**Base:** versão final da spec `minilab.work Frontend - Control Plane + Santo André Laboratory`  
**Alvo:** traduzir a UI atual para o modelo final sem reescrever o produto do zero  
**Instância:** Santo André Laboratory  
**Produto:** minilab.work  
**Natureza:** frontend / cockpit / pitwall / control plane  
**Regra:** preservar o que existe, corrigir identidade, escurecer/normalizar UI, explicitar fronteiras LogLine.

---

## 0. Decisão do delta

Este delta não transforma a aplicação em um novo produto.

Ele transforma a UI atual em:

```txt
minilab.work
Frontend and operational cockpit for Santo André Laboratory.
```

O objetivo é corrigir quatro coisas:

```txt
1. identidade
2. layout semântico
3. dark-mode cockpit
4. fronteiras operacionais LogLine
```

Não é objetivo deste delta implementar todo o LogLine Lab público.

Não é objetivo deste delta implementar toda a CLI/labd.

Não é objetivo deste delta tornar Hermes real se Hermes ainda não estiver integrado.

Não é objetivo deste delta fingir receipts, evidência, hooks ou runtime observation que ainda não existem.

Este delta deve mostrar ghosts honestos para o que ainda não está implementado.

---

## 1. Estado atual presumido

A UI atual já possui traços bons:

```txt
dark cockpit feel
control plane home
code lab surface
painéis escuros
ações primárias em azul
estado/policy com verde
estrutura próxima de workbench
módulos de gates/receipts/evidence em código
```

Mas ela ainda sofre de riscos:

```txt
identidade antiga de vibe coding
Dan Control Plane aparecendo como produto isolado
Santo André Laboratory não suficientemente central
Code Lab podendo parecer playground
chat podendo parecer centro do produto
light-mode leakage em componentes
ausência de Daily Lab State explícito
ausência de separação visual entre evidence, ghost, receipt e runtime success
ausência de Project Canon visível
ausência de CLI/labd boundary clara
```

O delta corrige esses riscos.

---

## 2. Resultado esperado

Ao final do delta, ao abrir a aplicação, deve ficar óbvio que:

```txt
Santo André Laboratory é o Lab.
minilab.work é o cockpit.
LogLine é o protocolo.
CLI/labd é o core operacional esperado.
Hermes é mão de execução quando integrado.
O frontend é superfície.
Evidence, ghosts e receipts são entidades visíveis.
```

A primeira impressão deve ser:

```txt
Santo André Laboratory is running.

This is a living LogLine Lab instance.
It has a clock.
It has ghosts.
It has evidence state.
It has machines.
It has next safe acts.
It does not pretend closure.
```

---

## 3. Fora de escopo

Este delta não deve:

```txt
implementar runtime real se não existir
simular receipts como se fossem reais
fechar ghosts automaticamente
promover canon
implementar passaporte/visa completo
implementar toda a CLI pública
implementar full Hermes apply mode
reescrever arquitetura de estado inteira
migrar todos os módulos se imports quebrarem
```

Quando algo não existir, a UI deve mostrar:

```txt
ghost
not integrated
not observed
pending implementation
```

Não usar:

```txt
done
verified
working
production-ready
```

sem evidência.

---

## 4. Princípio de implementação

A implementação deve ser incremental.

Ordem recomendada:

```txt
1. limpar pacote
2. corrigir identidade textual
3. consolidar dark mode
4. criar shell de layout pitwall
5. criar Daily Lab State fake-but-honest
6. conectar primitives existentes
7. criar páginas/abas semânticas
8. normalizar Code Lab
9. adicionar ghosts de integração
10. rodar lint/test/build
```

Fake data é aceitável apenas se marcada como:

```txt
mock
declared
planned
ghost
not runtime-observed
```

Nunca marcar mock como evidence.

---

## 5. Limpeza do pacote

Remover da árvore ativa:

```txt
__MACOSX/
.DS_Store
.next/
tsconfig.tsbuildinfo
.playwright-mcp/
logs temporários
screenshots soltos na raiz
artefatos de build
```

Mover screenshots para:

```txt
docs/assets/screenshots/
```

Atualizar `.gitignore`:

```gitignore
.next/
.DS_Store
__MACOSX/
*.tsbuildinfo
.playwright-mcp/
*.log
```

Preservar:

```txt
.env.example
src/control-plane ou src/dan primitives
lib/lab-events
src/engines
componentes UI existentes
testes existentes
```

---

## 6. Identidade do pacote

Atualizar `package.json`:

```json
{
  "name": "minilab-work"
}
```

Alternativa aceitável:

```json
{
  "name": "minilab-work-frontend"
}
```

Evitar:

```txt
vibe-coding-platform
dan-control-plane
logline-lab-kit
```

`dan-control-plane` pode aparecer como módulo interno, não como produto inteiro.

---

## 7. README delta

Trocar título principal para:

```txt
minilab.work
```

Subtítulo:

```txt
Frontend and operational cockpit for Santo André Laboratory.
```

README deve conter:

```txt
What this is
What this is not
Architecture boundary
Local development
Safety
Status
```

Texto mínimo:

```txt
minilab.work is the frontend and operational cockpit for Santo André Laboratory,
a concrete LogLine Lab instance.

It is not LogLine Foundation.
It is not the generic LogLine Lab kit.
It is not the semantic source of truth.
It is not the executor.

It displays, routes, prepares and calls operational backends.
LogLine Acts carry meaning.
CLI/labd operates.
Hermes executes admitted workorders when available.
Evidence supports.
Receipts close narrowly.
Ghosts preserve absence.
```

---

Substituir linguagem antiga:

```txt
Dan Control Plane
```

por linguagem final:

```txt
minilab.work
Santo André Laboratory
Lab Cockpit
Control Plane

```

Onde aparecer “Dan Control Plane”, usar preferencialmente:


Exemplo:

```txt
Dan Infrastructure Control Plane
```

mas dentro de `minilab.work`, não como produto separado.

Se não for possível criar todas agora, criar pelo menos:

e deixar links desabilitados com estado:

```txt
not implemented
```

## 10. Layout pitwall

Implementar layout base com três planos:

```txt
Left Rail
Center Surface
Right Rail
Bottom Strip
Top Bar
```

### Top Bar

Mostrar:

```txt
Santo André Laboratory
active interval
active lane
project canon
clock status
```

Mock inicial aceitável:

```txt
Santo André Laboratory

Lane: Cockpit
Project Canon: not connected
Clock: declared
```

### Left Rail

Abas:

```txt
Acts
Ghosts
Receipts
Experiments
Runtimes
Hooks
Canon
Reports
```

### Center

Superfície principal:

```txt
Daily Lab State
Code Lab
Operator Console
Machine Surface
```

### Right Rail

Radio / Translator:

```txt
I see...
I do not see...
This ghost remains...
The next safe act is...
```

### Bottom Strip

Evidence / Hooks / Gates:

```txt
evidence state
hook state
gate state
runtime envelope
secret redaction
```

## 11. Dark mode

A aplicação deve ser dark-mode nativa.

Criar/normalizar tokens em `app/globals.css`:

```css
:root {
  --background: ...;
  --foreground: ...;
  --panel: ...;
  --panel-muted: ...;
  --card: ...;
  --border: ...;
  --muted: ...;
  --muted-foreground: ...;
  --primary: ...;
  --primary-foreground: ...;
  --success: ...;
  --warning: ...;
  --destructive: ...;
  --ghost: ...;
}
```

Remover vazamentos:

```txt
bg-white
text-black
text-gray-900
border-gray-200
bg-slate-50
bg-neutral-50
default white input
default white dialog
default white popover
unstyled white code block
```

Substituir por classes/tokens escuros.

Design-alvo:

```txt
matte black
charcoal panels
low-contrast borders
blue primary actions
green for healthy/valid
amber for ghost/warning
red for rejected/destructive
compact cockpit typography
```

## 12. Daily Lab State - implementação mínima

Criar componente:

```txt
components/lab/DailyLabState.tsx
```

Deve mostrar cards:

```txt
Clock
Canon
Open Ghosts
Receipt Candidates
Stale Probes
Hook Failures
Machines Online
Last Evidence
Next Safe Act
```

Dados iniciais podem vir de mock explícito:

```ts
const dailyLabState = {
  source: "mock",
  evidence_state: "declared",
  runtime_observed: false
}
```

Mostrar badge:

```txt
declared / not runtime-observed
```

Nunca mostrar mock como verified.

Exemplo de conteúdo:

```txt
Santo André Laboratory is running.

Clock: declared
Canon: project-canon not connected
Open ghosts: 7
Receipt candidates: 2
Stale probes: 1
Mandatory hook failures: unknown
Machines online: unknown
Last evidence captured: not observed

Next safe act:
  connect Daily Lab State to labd or Current State projection
```

---


```txt
labd-interface-unimplemented

ghost-board-data-source-unconfirmed

hermes-runtime-not-integrated
secret-redaction-unverified
```

Ghost Board deve ser visualmente nobre, não rodapé de erro.

Frase:

```txt
Ghosts are preserved absence.
```

---

## 14. Evidence Strip - implementação mínima

```txt
components/lab/EvidenceStrip.tsx
```

Mostrar:

```txt
evidence_state
runtime_observed

stderr_hash
exit_code
diff_hash
artifact_refs
runtime_envelope
redaction_status
```

Se não houver execução:

```txt
No runtime evidence observed in this interval.
```

Não mostrar estado vazio como sucesso.

Estados visuais:

```txt
unknown = muted
declared = muted/blue
observed = blue
evidence_captured = green
verified = green strong
ghost = amber
rejected = red
```

---

```txt
No receipt-backed closure observed.
```

Mostrar bloqueios:

```txt
evidence missing
receipt profile missing
conformance unobserved
broad claim from narrow evidence
```

Nunca exibir:

```txt
Verified
Done
Closed
```

sem receipt refs.

## 20. Translator / Race Radio delta

Criar componente:

```txt
components/lab/RaceRadio.tsx
```

Mensagens devem usar formato:

```txt
I see...
I do not see...
This act claims...
This evidence supports...
This ghost remains...
The next safe act is...
```

Não usar:

```txt
I verified
I completed
It works
Trust me
```

Estado inicial sugerido:

```txt
I see Santo André Laboratory declared as the active Lab.
I do not see labd runtime evidence yet.
This ghost remains: daily-lab-state-projection-unimplemented.
The next safe act is to connect Current State projection or keep this panel marked declared.
```

Mostrar os quatro eixos:

```txt
artifact_state: drafted
evidence_state: declared

```

```txt
claim
artifact
evidence
trust
visibility
blockers
next allowed state
```

Bloquear salto visual:

```txt
generated → trusted-operational-consequence
```

## 22. Lab Events delta

Preservar `lib/lab-events/*`.

Se já existir pipeline, não reescrever.

```txt
components/lab/LabEventsPanel.tsx
```

Mostrar eventos como observações, não receipts.

Campos:

```txt

```

Se `secret_redacted !== true`, mostrar warning forte.

## 23. Módulos de domínio a preservar

Não achatar em `utils`.

Preservar:

```txt
contracts.ts
evaluatePolicy.ts
gateLifecycle.ts
receiptLifecycle.ts
actionRegistry.ts
minilabUniverse.ts
minilabUniverseSeed.ts
validatePolicy.ts
engineRegistry.ts
localShellEngine.ts
vercelSandboxEngine.ts
dopplerConfigEngine.ts
lib/lab-events/*
```

```txt
1. manter se mover for arriscado
2. mover para src/control-plane/ com imports corrigidos
```

Não mover para `lib/utils`.

Esses módulos são primitives institucionais.

## 27. Regras de texto na UI

Substituir frases ruins:

```txt
AI completed this
verified
done
production ready
ship it
```

por frases LogLine-safe:

```txt
candidate prepared
runtime not observed
evidence missing
receipt blocked
ghost opened
ready for review
workorder required
verification required
```

Se uma ação ainda não está conectada:

```txt
Not connected to labd.
This action is staged only.
```

---

## 28. Segurança visual

Nenhum componente deve renderizar:

```txt
.env content
secret values
tokens
service role key
private credentials
raw process.env
```

Se existir área de config:

```txt
show secret names only
show presence/absence
show redaction status
```

Exemplo:

```txt
SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY: present / value hidden / server-only
```

---

## 29. Critérios de aceite do delta

O delta é aceitável quando:

```txt
1. README diz minilab.work e Santo André Laboratory.
2. Home mostra Daily Lab State.
3. Santo André Laboratory é identidade principal.
4. UI está dark-mode sem painéis brancos acidentais.
5. Code Lab aparece como governed workbench.
6. Ghost Board existe ou ghosts aparecem na Home.
7. Evidence Strip existe ou estado de evidência aparece claramente.
8. Receipts não são confundidos com runtime success.
9. Project Canon aparece ao menos como painel/rota staged.
10. CLI/labd boundary é explícita.
11. Ações não conectadas aparecem como staged/ghost.
12. Primitives existentes de gate/receipt/policy/lab-events são preservadas.
13. Build/lint/test foram rodados ou falhas foram registradas como ghosts.
```

:::writing{variant="document" id="91372"}
# minilab.work Frontend - Delta 02 Implementation Spec

## Current State Projection Adapter

**Status:** implementation delta  
**Base:** Delta 01 UI identity transformation  
**Target:** connect Daily Lab State to the first real/read-only Current State projection  
**Product:** minilab.work  
**Instance:** Santo André Laboratory  
**Rule:** observe before claiming; project before closing; ghost missing integrations honestly.

---

## 0. Decision

Delta 02 connects the frontend to a first Current State source.

The goal is not to implement full labd, Hermes, receipts, hooks, or runtime execution.

The goal is narrower:

```txt
Daily Lab State must stop being only declared_static_seed
and become a read-only projection from one observable source,
while preserving declared/mock fallback and ghosts.
```

Accepted first sources:

```txt
1. local current-state JSON file
2. generated current-state JSON artifact
3. Supabase audit/current-state projection
4. labd status endpoint
```

Preferred first implementation:

```txt
local file projection first
then database/labd later
```

Because file projection is simple, reviewable, deterministic, and does not pretend runtime integration.

---

## 1. What this delta closes

This delta may close:

```txt
daily-lab-state-projection-unimplemented
```

only if the frontend reads a real source artifact instead of hardcoded component data.

It may narrow but not close:

```txt
labd-interface-unimplemented
hermes-runtime-not-integrated
evidence-strip-runtime-integration-missing
receipt-review-lane-unimplemented
mandatory-hooks-enforcement-unimplemented
```

It should create or preserve ghosts for every missing backend.

---

## 2. Source hierarchy

Current State adapter must resolve sources in explicit order.

Recommended order:

```txt
1. labd observed state
2. database projection observed state
3. local file projection observed state
4. declared static seed
5. ghost
```

For Delta 02, implement at least:

```txt
local file projection observed state
→ declared static seed fallback
→ ghost on failure
```

Do not skip directly to fake labd.

---

## 3. Projection status model

Create a status model that prevents fake confidence.

File:

```txt
src/santo-andre/currentStateTypes.ts
```

Suggested types:

```ts
export type ProjectionStatus =
  | "declared_static_seed"
  | "file_projection_observed"
  | "database_projection_observed"
  | "labd_observed"
  | "ghost";

export type EvidenceState =
  | "unknown"
  | "planned"
  | "declared"
  | "observed"
  | "evidence_captured"
  | "verified"
  | "ghost"
  | "retired"
  | "superseded";

export type RuntimeObservationState =
  | "not_runtime_observed"
  | "operator_reported"
  | "file_observed"
  | "database_observed"
  | "labd_observed"
  | "hermes_observed";
```

Rule:

```txt
projection_status says where the state came from.
evidence_state says how strong the claim is.
runtime_observation_state says whether runtime contact exists.
```

---

## 4. Current State shape

Create normalized interface:

```ts
export interface CurrentStateProjection {
  projection_status: ProjectionStatus;
  evidence_state: EvidenceState;
  runtime_observation_state: RuntimeObservationState;

  lab: {
    id: string;
    name: string;
    status: string;
    clock_status: string;
  };

  canon: {
    foundation_ref?: string | null;
    lab_profile_ref?: string | null;
    project_canon_ref?: string | null;
    project_canon_hash?: string | null;
  };

  counts: {
    open_ghosts: number | null;
    receipt_candidates: number | null;
    stale_probes: number | null;
    mandatory_hook_failures: number | null;
    machines_online: number | null;
    machines_total: number | null;
  };

  last_evidence: {
    captured_at?: string | null;
    evidence_ref?: string | null;
    summary?: string | null;
  };

  next_safe_act: {
    label: string;
    reason?: string;
    target?: string;
  };

  ghosts: Array<{
    ghost_key: string;
    what_missing: string;
    why_it_matters: string;
    blocks?: string;
    next_act?: string;
    status: "open" | "carried" | "narrowed" | "closed";
  }>;

  source: {
    kind: "file" | "database" | "labd" | "static_seed" | "ghost";
    ref: string;
    observed_at: string;
    hash?: string | null;
  };
}
```

---

## 5. Local projection file

Create:

```txt
data/current-state/santo-andre.current-state.json
```

Initial content should be honest:

```json
{
  "projection_status": "file_projection_observed",
  "evidence_state": "declared",
  "runtime_observation_state": "file_observed",
  "lab": {
    "id": "santo-andre-laboratory",
    "name": "Santo André Laboratory",
    "status": "declared",
    "clock_status": "declared"
  },
  "canon": {
    "foundation_ref": null,
    "lab_profile_ref": null,
    "project_canon_ref": null,
    "project_canon_hash": null
  },
  "counts": {
    "open_ghosts": 10,
    "receipt_candidates": 0,
    "stale_probes": null,
    "mandatory_hook_failures": null,
    "machines_online": null,
    "machines_total": null
  },
  "last_evidence": {
    "captured_at": null,
    "evidence_ref": null,
    "summary": "No runtime evidence captured from labd/Hermes yet."
  },
  "next_safe_act": {
    "label": "Connect Current State projection to labd or database source.",
    "reason": "Frontend is currently reading a local projection artifact.",
    "target": "current-state-adapter"
  },
  "ghosts": [
    {
      "ghost_key": "labd-interface-unimplemented",
      "what_missing": "No labd status endpoint is connected.",
      "why_it_matters": "Frontend cannot observe live Lab state.",
      "blocks": "runtime-observed Daily Lab State",
      "next_act": "implement labd status endpoint or adapter",
      "status": "open"
    },
    {
      "ghost_key": "hermes-runtime-not-integrated",
      "what_missing": "No Hermes workorder execution is connected.",
      "why_it_matters": "Operator Console cannot execute admitted workorders.",
      "blocks": "runtime execution evidence",
      "next_act": "define Hermes read-only workorder integration",
      "status": "open"
    }
  ],
  "source": {
    "kind": "file",
    "ref": "data/current-state/santo-andre.current-state.json",
    "observed_at": "2026-05-28T00:00:00Z",
    "hash": null
  }
}
```

Important:

```txt
This file is not canon.
This file is not receipt.
This file is not runtime proof.
This file is a projection artifact.
```

---

## 6. Adapter implementation

Create:

```txt
src/santo-andre/currentStateAdapter.ts
```

Responsibilities:

```txt
read local current-state JSON
validate basic shape
normalize missing values
fallback to declared static seed
return ghost projection if read/parse fails
```

Suggested API:

```ts
import type { CurrentStateProjection } from "./currentStateTypes";

export async function getCurrentStateProjection(): Promise<CurrentStateProjection> {
  // 1. Try file projection.
  // 2. If unavailable, return declared static seed.
  // 3. If seed unavailable, return ghost projection.
}
```

Required behavior:

```txt
Never throw raw error into UI.
Convert missing source into ghost.
Never silently replace failed source with success-looking mock.
```

---

## 7. Optional file hash

If simple to implement, compute SHA-256 of the JSON content.

If not implemented, set:

```json
"hash": null
```

and preserve ghost:

```txt
current-state-file-hash-missing
```

Do not fake hash.

instead of importing hardcoded state directly.

and call from client component.

Preferred:

```txt
server-side read first
client fetch only if needed
```

to receive ghosts from `CurrentStateProjection`.

No ghosts in current

Sim. Você está certo. Eu errei feio nesse ponto.

**Nada de `data/current-state/*.json` como fonte operacional.** Isso reintroduz exatamente o tipo de pseudo-ledger/local-file truth que a doutrina estava tentando matar.

A correção é:

```txt
LogLine Acts go to Supabase. Period.

ops.logline_acts is the semantic write spine.
Everything else is projection.
```

Isso está diretamente alinhado com o Practice Profile: “every semantic write” é LogLine Act; `ops.logline_acts` é o spine semântico; `registry.*`, `audit.*`, `evidence.*`, `receipts.*` e `lab_observability.*` são projeções. `12_minilab_logline_practice_profile_decisions.md`

Então o Delta 02 correto não é “Current State JSON Adapter”. É:

**document: **

# minilab.work Frontend - Delta 02 Implementation Spec

## Supabase LogLine Act Spine Adapter

**Status:** corrected implementation delta  
**Base:** Delta 01 UI identity transformation  
**Target:** connect minilab.work to Supabase as LogLine act spine + projection surface  
**Product:** minilab.work  
**Instance:** Santo André Laboratory  
**Non-negotiable rule:** LogLine Acts go to Supabase. Period.

---

## 0. Correction

Reject the previous local JSON projection idea.

There must be no operational `data/current-state/*.json` source.

There must be no local pseudo-ledger.

There must be no filesystem “current state” standing beside Supabase.

The operational rule is:

```txt
All semantic writes go to ops.logline_acts.
Supabase/Postgres stores the act spine.
Views/tables under registry.*, audit.*, evidence.*, receipts.*, lab_observability.* are projections.
The frontend reads projections.
The frontend emits admitted/candidate acts only through server-side admitted paths.
```

---

## 1. What this delta does

Delta 02 connects the frontend to Supabase in read-first mode.

It must:

```txt
1. read Daily Lab State from Supabase projections;
2. read ghosts from Supabase projections;
3. read receipts/evidence/projected state from Supabase when available;
4. preserve ghosts when projection tables/views are missing or empty;
5. prepare a server-side path for emitting LogLine Acts into ops.logline_acts;
6. avoid direct client writes to semantic or projection tables.
```

It does not need to implement full Hermes/labd yet.

It does not need to close receipts.

It does not need to enforce all hooks.

It does need to stop pretending local files are operational state.

---

## 2. Source hierarchy

For minilab.work runtime:

```txt
1. Supabase ops.logline_acts
   semantic write spine

2. Supabase projection views/tables
   audit.*
   registry.*
   evidence.*
   receipts.*
   lab_observability.*

3. UI declared fallback
   only for rendering empty states and ghosts

4. Storybook/dev fixtures
   allowed only outside operational runtime
```

Forbidden:

```txt
local JSON as current state source
local JSON as ghost registry
local JSON as evidence source
local JSON as receipt source
filesystem ledger
mock data displayed as observed
client-side direct semantic writes
direct writes into projection tables
```

---

## 3. Supabase client boundary

Create:

```txt
src/supabase/server.ts
src/supabase/client.ts
```

Rules:

```txt
browser client:
  may read public/safe projections only

server client:
  may use service role only in server-only modules
  never expose service role to browser
  may call RPC/server action to emit acts

frontend components:
  receive typed data from server loaders/actions
  never import service role client
```

Required environment variables:

```txt
NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL
NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY
SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY
```

Safety:

```txt
SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY must be server-only.
No secret values in browser payloads.
No env dump.
No raw process.env rendering.
```

---

## 4. Read adapter

Create:

```txt
src/santo-andre/supabaseCurrentStateAdapter.ts
```

This adapter reads from Supabase projections.

Initial read targets:

```txt
audit.v_mobile_today
lab_observability.current_state
lab_observability.ghosts
registry.entities
registry.runtimes
receipts.*
evidence.*
```

But it must tolerate missing tables/views.

If a projection is missing:

```txt
return ghost:
  projection-missing:<projection_name>
```

If a projection exists but is empty:

```txt
return state:
  evidence_state: observed_empty_projection
```

Do not silently replace missing database state with fake local state.

---

## 5. Daily Lab State source

Daily Lab State should be built from Supabase.

Preferred first query:

```sql
select * from audit.v_mobile_today;
```

If `audit.v_mobile_today` exists and returns a row:

```txt
projection_status = "supabase_projection_observed"
evidence_state = "observed"
runtime_observation_state = "database_observed"
```

If it does not exist:

```txt
projection_status = "ghost"
evidence_state = "ghost"
ghost = "audit.v_mobile_today-missing"
```

If it exists but returns no row:

```txt
projection_status = "supabase_projection_observed"
evidence_state = "observed_empty_projection"
ghost = "daily-state-empty"
```

The UI must display this distinction.

---

## 6. Projection status model

Create:

```txt
src/santo-andre/currentStateTypes.ts
```

Use:

```ts
export type ProjectionStatus =
  | "supabase_projection_observed"
  | "supabase_projection_empty"
  | "supabase_projection_missing"
  | "supabase_connection_failed"
  | "declared_ui_fallback"
  | "ghost";

export type EvidenceState =
  | "unknown"
  | "planned"
  | "declared"
  | "observed"
  | "observed_empty_projection"
  | "evidence_captured"
  | "verified"
  | "ghost"
  | "retired"
  | "superseded";

export type RuntimeObservationState =
  | "not_runtime_observed"
  | "database_observed"
  | "runtime_observed"
  | "hermes_observed"
  | "labd_observed";
```

Important distinction:

```txt
database_observed ≠ runtime_observed
projection observed ≠ evidence captured
evidence captured ≠ receipt closed
```

---

## 7. Normalized Daily Lab State

Create normalized shape:

```ts
export interface DailyLabStateProjection {
  projection_status: ProjectionStatus;
  evidence_state: EvidenceState;
  runtime_observation_state: RuntimeObservationState;

  source: {
    kind: "supabase_projection" | "supabase_error" | "declared_ui_fallback";
    ref: string;
    observed_at: string;
  };

  lab: {
    id: "santo-andre-laboratory";
    name: "Santo André Laboratory";
    status: string;
    clock_status: string;
  };

  counts: {
    entities_active: number | null;
    entities_ghost: number | null;
    logline_acts_24h: number | null;
    lab_ghosts_open: number | null;
    unverified_links: number | null;
    labs_strange: number | null;
    releases_pending: number | null;
    receipt_candidates: number | null;
    evidence_items: number | null;
  };

  ghosts: Array<{
    ghost_key: string;
    what_missing: string;
    why_it_matters: string;
    blocks?: string;
    next_act?: string;
    status: "open" | "carried" | "narrowed" | "closed";
  }>;

  next_safe_act: {
    label: string;
    reason?: string;
    target?: string;
  };
}
```

In `app/page.tsx`, prefer a server-side loader:

```ts
const dailyLabState = await getDailyLabStateFromSupabase();
```

Do not fetch Supabase directly from a client component unless using safe anon/RLS projections.

Recommended files:

```txt
src/santo-andre/getDailyLabState.ts
src/santo-andre/supabaseCurrentStateAdapter.ts
components/lab/DailyLabState.tsx
```

## 9. UI badges

Daily Lab State must show:

```txt
Source: Supabase
Projection: audit.v_mobile_today
Projection status: observed / missing / empty / failed
Evidence state: observed / ghost / observed_empty_projection
Runtime: database_observed / not_runtime_observed
```

Examples:

```txt
Projection observed from Supabase.
Runtime not observed.
No receipt closure claimed.
```

or:

```txt
Supabase projection missing.
Ghost opened: audit.v_mobile_today-missing.
```

---

## 10. Ghost handling

If Supabase connection fails:

```txt
ghost: supabase-connection-failed
```

If `audit.v_mobile_today` is missing:

```txt
ghost: audit-v-mobile-today-missing
```

If `ops.logline_acts` cannot be read by the server path:

```txt
ghost: ops-logline-acts-unreadable
```

If service role is missing:

```txt
ghost: supabase-service-role-missing
```

If anon key/RLS blocks expected safe projection read:

```txt
ghost: projection-rls-blocked
```

No missing Supabase state should be hidden behind mock.

---

## 11. Act emission path

Create a server-only action or API route:

```txt
app/api/logline/acts/route.ts
```

or server action:

```txt
emitLogLineActCandidate()
```

Initial mode:

```txt
candidate-only
```

Allowed:

```txt
insert into ops.logline_acts
```

Forbidden:

```txt
direct insert into registry.*
direct insert into audit.*
direct insert into evidence.*
direct insert into receipts.*
direct insert into lab_observability.*
client-side semantic write
```

Every write payload must be LogLine-shaped:

```txt
who
did
this
when
confirmed_by
if_ok
if_doubt
if_not
status
```

Runtime envelope fields may be included according to current schema/practice.

---

## 12. Database write law

All semantic writes:

```txt
ops.logline_acts
```

All read models:

```txt
projections
```

Allowed write target for this delta:

```txt
ops.logline_acts
```

Allowed read targets:

```txt
audit.*
registry.*
evidence.*
receipts.*
lab_observability.*
```

Projection tables should not be directly mutated by frontend code.

If projection data is missing, emit or propose a LogLine Act that would allow a projector to create the state.

## 13. UI action mapping

Buttons should map to act candidates, not direct mutations.

Examples:

```txt
Open Ghost
→ propose/emit LogLine Act:
  did = open_ghost

Prepare Receipt Candidate
→ propose/emit LogLine Act:
  did = prepare_receipt_candidate

Register Runtime
→ propose/emit LogLine Act:
  did = register_runtime

Observe LAB Heartbeat
→ propose/emit LogLine Act:
  did = observe_runtime
```

No button should directly write projection rows.

## 14. Current State screen behavior

If Supabase returns `audit.v_mobile_today`:

```txt
show Daily Lab State from projection
```

If Supabase returns ghosts:

```txt
show Ghost Board from projection
```

If evidence/receipts projections are absent:

```txt
show ghost cards
```

If act spine is reachable but projections are missing:

```txt
show:
  Act spine reachable.
  Projection missing.
  Next safe act: create/project audit view from ops.logline_acts.
```

If Supabase is unreachable:

```txt
show:
  Supabase unavailable.
  No operational state observed.
  UI fallback only.
```

## 15. Acceptance criteria

Delta 02 is accepted only if:

```txt
1. No local JSON current-state source exists.
2. Daily Lab State attempts Supabase read.
3. audit.v_mobile_today is used if available.
4. Missing Supabase projections become ghosts.
5. UI labels database observation separately from runtime observation.
6. Act emission path targets ops.logline_acts only.
7. Projection tables are read-only from frontend perspective.
8. Service role is server-only.
9. Missing backend state is not replaced by fake successful state.
10. Build/lint/typecheck pass or failures are ghosted.
```

```txt
Queries tested:
Command receipts:
Ghosts:
What this closes:
What this does not close:

```

```txt
query result or error for audit.v_mobile_today
query result or error for ops.logline_acts read path
build output
lint/typecheck output
```

## 17. Final correction sentence

```txt
Delta 02 does not add a local current-state file.

Delta 02 connects minilab.work to the Supabase LogLine act spine:
ops.logline_acts for semantic writes,
Supabase projections for read surfaces,
and ghosts for every missing projection or runtime path.
```

Essa é a correção. Sem ambiguidade.

O motivo técnico/institucional: `Current State` é uma visão operacional, não canon/receipt/proof, e deve impedir reinício por memória, arquivos soltos ou interpretação de LLM. `06_current_state_v_0.md` O Source of Truth Map já proíbe “file exists, therefore canonical” e “database row exists, therefore authorized”; a fonte precisa ter classe, escopo e evidence state. `03_source_of_truth_map.md` Então: **Supabase sim; local JSON não.**

## Prompt:
5/28/2026, 10:15:46 PM

E O QUE EH O BACKND´~

## Response:
5/28/2026, 10:15:49 PM

O backend **não é um backend de app clássico**. É um **stack operacional** com Supabase como spine/memória/projeção e runtimes separados para admissão, execução e evidência.

A forma correta:

```txt
Frontend:
  minilab.work
  pitwall / cockpit / UI

Backend:
  Supabase/Postgres
  + server API do minilab.work
  + projectors
  + Constitutional Runtime / admission
  + Authority/Gates/Execution Windows
  + Hermes
  + LAB runners
  + Evidence/Receipt/Ghost projectors
```

Mais curto ainda:

```txt
Backend = Supabase act spine + server-side control endpoints + runtimes.
```

## O núcleo

O backend começa em:

```txt
Supabase
  ops.logline_acts
```

Ponto. Todo semantic write vai para `ops.logline_acts`. O Practice Profile crava isso: não há business objects nativos no core, só LogLine Acts admitidos e projeções; `ops.logline_acts` é o semantic write spine, enquanto `registry.*`, `audit.*`, `evidence.*`, `receipts.*` e `lab_observability.*` são projeções. `12_minilab_logline_practice_profile_decisions.md`

Então:

```txt
ops.logline_acts = write spine
registry.* = identity/runtime/capability projections
audit.* = safe read projections
evidence.* = observation/evidence projections
receipts.* = scoped-closure projections
lab_observability.* = LAB/runtime state projections
```

## O que NÃO é backend

Não é:

```txt
Next.js state
React components
local JSON
Zustand store
mock seed
chat transcript
README
filesystem ledger
```

Essas coisas podem ajudar a renderizar, testar ou explicar. Mas não são backend operacional.

## A arquitetura real

```txt
minilab.work frontend
  ↓
Next.js server/API layer
  ↓
Supabase/Postgres
  - ops.logline_acts
  - registry.*
  - audit.*
  - evidence.*
  - receipts.*
  - lab_observability.*
  ↓
Constitutional Runtime / admission
  ↓
Authority / Gates / Execution Windows
  ↓
Hermes workorders
  ↓
LAB runners / machines / runtimes
  ↓
Execution Reports / Evidence Records
  ↓
Supabase projections / receipts / ghosts
  ↓
frontend reads state
```

A Vertical Runtime Doctrine dá a linha: intent → office → process → LogLine candidate → Constitutional Runtime admission → Authority/Gate → Dispatch packet → Hermes workorder → LAB execution → evidence return → receipt/ghost → projection → Morning State. `09_vertical_runtime_doctrine.md`

## Então o backend tem 5 partes

### 1. Supabase/Postgres

É o backend de memória e projeção.

Responsável por:

```txt
guardar acts
indexar receipts
projetar registry
projetar audit/mobile views
projetar ghosts
projetar evidence
projetar runtime/LAB state
```

Mas Supabase **não governa**. O banco projeta acts; não inventa significado nem fecha prova. O próprio profile diz: o act é conteúdo, envelope é proveniência, runtime registry é capacidade, projector é significado. `12_minilab_logline_practice_profile_decisions.md`

### 2. Next.js server/API

É a borda segura entre frontend e Supabase/runtimes.

Responsável por:

```txt
server-only Supabase client
service role nunca no browser
read loaders para audit.*, registry.*, evidence.*, receipts.*
server actions/API routes para propor/emitir LogLine Acts
validação de payload
normalização de erros em ghosts
```

O browser não escreve direto em `ops.logline_acts` com poder solto.

### 3. Projectors

São o backend que transforma acts em mundos legíveis.

```txt
ops.logline_acts
  → audit.v_mobile_today
  → registry.entities
  → registry.runtimes
  → ghost board
  → evidence strip
  → receipt review
  → daily lab state
```

Projector pode ser:

```txt
SQL view
SQL function
Edge Function
server job
Rust/TypeScript worker
manual bootstrap projector no começo
```

Mas a regra é invariável:

```txt
projection renders state.
projection does not create canon.
projection does not authorize execution.
projection does not close proof.
```

Isso está explícito na Vertical Runtime Doctrine. `09_vertical_runtime_doctrine.md`

### 4. Constitutional Runtime / Authority

Esse é o backend de admissão e consequência.

Responsável por:

```txt
validar candidate act
admitir / rejeitar / ghostar
classificar autoridade
decidir se precisa Dan
decidir se precisa execution window
decidir se vira dispatch/workorder
```

Sem isso, vira CRUD com vocabulário bonito.

### 5. Hermes + LAB runners

Esse é o backend de execução.

Hermes recebe **workorders**, não chat. O contrato é cristalino: Hermes executa trabalho admitido, não governa; o caminho correto é intent → process → dispatch packet → runtime admission → authority classification → Hermes workorder → LAB execution → evidence packet → receipt/ghost/projection. `10_hermes_dispatch_and_execution_contract.md`

Hermes retorna:

```txt
execution report
stdout/stderr refs
exit code
artifact hashes
runtime observations
ghosts
evidence packet
```

E isso volta para Supabase como LogLine-shaped acts/evidence projections. Evidence não vira receipt automaticamente; receipt candidate só depois de evidência e escopo. `10_hermes_dispatch_and_execution_contract.md`

## Nome simples para a spec

Eu chamaria:

```txt
minilab.work Backend Contract
```

Com subtítulo:

```txt
Supabase LogLine Spine + Runtime Control Boundary
```

## Frase final

```txt
O backend do minilab.work é Supabase como LogLine act spine,
mais uma camada server-side que lê projeções e emite acts,
mais runtimes separados para admitir, executar, observar e retornar evidência.

Frontend mostra.
Supabase lembra.
Projectors tornam legível.
Runtime admite.
Authority governa consequência.
Hermes executa.
LABs dão corpo.
Evidence volta.
Receipts fecham.
Ghosts preservam.
```

Então o próximo delta correto é:

```txt
Delta 02 - Supabase Backend Adapter
```

Não “current-state JSON”. Não “frontend store”. Não “mock backend”.

**Supabase primeiro. `ops.logline_acts` primeiro. Projeções depois.**

Sim. Você tem razão - eu desviei para `minilab.work`, frontend, backend, adapter. **O centro agora é o Lab Kit.** Sem UI. Sem JSON local. Sem “talvez backend”. O kit tem que instalar uma prática operacional de LogLine: canon carregado, Supabase como act spine, CLI/labd, manifest, projectors, ghosts, evidence, receipts, clock, hooks, dispatch, Hermes boundary. Isso segue diretamente o Practice Profile, a Vertical Runtime Doctrine, o Hermes Contract, o Current State, o Source of Truth Map e o Modus Operandi de Santo André. `12_minilab_logline_practice_profile_decisions.md` `09_vertical_runtime_doctrine.md` `10_hermes_dispatch_and_execution_contract.md` `06_current_state_v_0.md` `03_source_of_truth_map.md` `11_santo-andre-lab-modus-operandi-doc-11-confirmed-by-witness-patch-v2.md`

Aqui está a versão correta:

**document: **

# LogLine Lab Kit - Spec de Produto, Instalação e Runtime v0

**Status:** spec final inicial / implementation target  
**Nome:** LogLine Lab Kit  
**Função:** kit operacional para instanciar um LogLine Lab real  
**Primeira instância-alvo:** Santo André Laboratory  
**UI opcional:** minilab.work  
**Regra-mãe:** LogLine Acts go to Supabase. Period.

---

## 0. Definição

O **LogLine Lab Kit** é o pacote instalável que permite criar um laboratório operacional baseado em LogLine.

Ele fornece:

```txt
canon loader
Supabase act spine
CLI
labd
manifest
runtime registry
projectors
ghost registry
evidence registry
receipt preparation
lab clock
mandatory hooks
process/dispatch contracts
Hermes workorder boundary
report generation
conformance hooks
study benches
```

O kit não é frontend.

O kit não é dashboard.

O kit não é minilab.work.

O kit não é Santo André Laboratory.

O kit é a infraestrutura mínima para que qualquer pessoa, instituição, laboratório ou comunidade possa estudar e construir com LogLine.

Forma curta:

```txt
LogLine Foundation is the grammar.
LogLine Lab Kit is the operational kit.
A Lab instance declares local practice.
Supabase stores the act spine.
CLI/labd operate the Lab.
Frontends are optional surfaces.
```

---

## 1. Decisão não negociável

Para este kit v0:

```txt
LogLine Acts go to Supabase.
```

O spine semântico é:

```txt
ops.logline_acts
```

Todo semantic write entra como LogLine Act.

Todo o resto é projeção.

```txt
registry.*
audit.*
evidence.*
receipts.*
lab_observability.*
authz.*
workorders.*
```

são superfícies derivadas, índices, views, projeções, registries ou estados operacionais reconstruíveis.

Proibido:

```txt
local JSON ledger
filesystem current-state ledger
frontend store como fonte operacional
mock state promovido a verdade
direct semantic writes into projection tables
receipt sem evidence
runtime success como closure
```

---

## 2. O que o Kit entrega

O kit entrega quatro coisas:

```txt
1. instalação
2. spine
3. runtime operacional
4. disciplina de estudo
```

### 2.1 Instalação

O kit deve instalar ou inicializar:

```txt
Supabase schema
LogLine schemas
CLI
labd
manifest
projectors
seed acts
doctor checks
default lab profile
```

### 2.2 Spine

O kit estabelece:

```txt
ops.logline_acts
```

como fonte de escrita semântica.

### 2.3 Runtime operacional

O kit fornece:

```txt
logline-lab CLI
labd daemon/API
projector runner
clock runner
hook runner
ghost/evidence/receipt commands
dispatch/workorder preparation
```

### 2.4 Disciplina de estudo

O kit fornece benches para estudar:

```txt
acts
runtimes
engines
projections
ghosts
receipts
intervals
experiments
AI-to-act translation
promotion control
what runs natively above software
```

---

## 3. O que o Kit não entrega

O kit não entrega obrigatoriamente:

```txt
frontend
minilab.work
Santo André branding
Dan’s infra
full Hermes implementation
full passkey auth
public website
LLM provider
local GPU runtime
production deployment
```

Essas coisas são overlays, adapters ou instâncias.

O kit deve rodar sem frontend.

O kit deve ser operável por CLI.

---

## 4. Camadas

```txt
LogLine Foundation
  canon, grammar, conformance, receipt discipline

LogLine Lab Kit
  CLI, labd, manifest, Supabase spine, projectors, hooks, ghosts, evidence, receipts, reports

Lab Instance
  Santo André Laboratory, community lab, company lab, personal lab

Local Overlay
  Dan/minilab.work, institution-specific policy, machines, identities, credentials, UX

Frontend
  optional cockpit: minilab.work or other UI
```

---
