## 6. Supabase schema mínimo

### 6.1 ops.logline_acts

Este é o spine.

```sql
create schema if not exists ops;

create table if not exists ops.logline_acts (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),

  who text not null,
  did text not null,
  this jsonb not null,
  "when" timestamptz not null default now(),
  confirmed_by jsonb not null default '{}'::jsonb,
  if_ok jsonb not null default '{}'::jsonb,
  if_doubt jsonb not null default '{}'::jsonb,
  if_not jsonb not null default '{}'::jsonb,
  status text not null,

  runtime_envelope jsonb not null default '{}'::jsonb,

  tuple_hash text,
  content_hash text,
  previous_act_refs text[] not null default '{}',

  evidence_state text not null default 'declared',
  promotion_state text not null default 'candidate',

  created_at timestamptz not null default now()
);
```

Regra:

```txt
Only LogLine-shaped semantic writes land here.
```

---

### 6.2 registry.*

```sql
create schema if not exists registry;
```

Projeções mínimas:

```txt
registry.entities
registry.runtimes
registry.links
registry.passports
registry.visas
registry.auth_bindings
```

Regra:

```txt
Identity is addressability.
Identity is not authority.
```

---

### 6.3 audit.*

```sql
create schema if not exists audit;
```

Views mínimas:

```txt
audit.v_mobile_today
audit.v_daily_lab_state
audit.v_open_ghosts
audit.v_receipt_candidates
audit.v_recent_acts
```

Regra:

```txt
audit.* is safe read projection.
```

---

### 6.4 lab_observability.*

```sql
create schema if not exists lab_observability;
```

Projeções:

```txt
lab_observability.current_state
lab_observability.ghosts
lab_observability.heartbeats
lab_observability.runtime_status
lab_observability.machine_state
```

---

### 6.5 evidence.*

```sql
create schema if not exists evidence;
```

Projeções:

```txt
evidence.records
evidence.artifacts
evidence.runtime_observations
evidence.command_outputs
```

---

### 6.6 receipts.*

```sql
create schema if not exists receipts;
```

Projeções:

```txt
receipts.index
receipts.candidates
receipts.blocked
receipts.closed
receipts.rejected
```

---

### 6.7 workorders.*

```sql
create schema if not exists workorders;
```

Projeções:

```txt
workorders.dispatch_packets
workorders.hermes_workorders
workorders.execution_reports
```

---

## 7. Manifest

Todo Lab deve declarar um manifest.

Arquivo:

```txt
lab.manifest.yaml
```

Shape:

```yaml
manifest_version: 1

lab:
  id: santo-andre-laboratory
  name: Santo André Laboratory
  kind: logline_lab_instance
  steward: Dan Voulez
  public_status: mixed

loads:
  foundation: logline.foundation@1.0.0
  lab_profile: logline-lab.practice@0.1.0
  local_overlay: santo-andre.practice@0.1.0

supabase:
  project_ref_env: SUPABASE_PROJECT_REF
  url_env: NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL
  anon_key_env: NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY
  service_role_env: SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY
  semantic_write: ops.logline_acts

rules:
  semantic_writes_go_to: ops.logline_acts
  runtime_envelope_required: true
  projections_are_read_models: true
  ghosts_are_first_class: true
  receipts_require_evidence: true
  frontend_is_optional: true

schemas:
  act: schemas/logline-act.schema.json
  runtime_envelope: schemas/runtime-envelope.schema.json
  dispatch_packet: schemas/dispatch-packet.schema.json
  workorder: schemas/hermes-workorder.schema.json
  execution_report: schemas/execution-report.schema.json

projectors:
  - audit.v_mobile_today
  - registry.entities
  - registry.runtimes
  - lab_observability.current_state
  - evidence.records
  - receipts.index
  - lab_observability.ghosts

clock:
  schedule: clock/schedules/default.lab-clock.yaml

hooks:
  - hooks/default/after_operator_edit.run_verification_plan.v1.yaml
  - hooks/default/before_receipt_review.require_evidence_refs.v1.yaml
  - hooks/default/before_publication.require_claim_refs.v1.yaml

benches:
  - dialogue-observatory
  - interval-workbench
  - runtime-observatory
  - projector-lab
  - promotion-control
```

---

## 8. CLI

Binário:

```bash
logline-lab
```

Comandos mínimos:

```bash
logline-lab init
logline-lab doctor
logline-lab status
logline-lab canon status
logline-lab act emit
logline-lab act get
logline-lab ghost list
logline-lab ghost open
logline-lab evidence add
logline-lab receipt prepare
logline-lab report generate
logline-lab projector run
logline-lab hook run
logline-lab clock tick
logline-lab dispatch prepare
logline-lab workorder prepare
```

### 8.1 init

```bash
logline-lab init --manifest manifests/santo-andre.manifest.example.yaml
```

Faz:

```txt
validate manifest
check env
connect Supabase
run migrations
seed lab registration acts
open initial ghosts
run doctor
```

### 8.2 doctor

```bash
logline-lab doctor
```

Verifica:

```txt
Supabase connection
ops.logline_acts exists
projection schemas exist
required views exist
service role server-only env present
anon key present
manifest valid
clock config valid
hooks parse
projectors registered
```

### 8.3 act emit

```bash
logline-lab act emit --file act.json
```

Insere em:

```txt
ops.logline_acts
```

Nunca em projection table.

### 8.4 status

```bash
logline-lab status
```

Lê:

```txt
audit.v_mobile_today
lab_observability.current_state
lab_observability.ghosts
receipts.candidates
evidence.records
```

Se não existir, ghosta.

---

## 9. labd

`labd` é o daemon/API local ou server-side do Lab.

Ele é opcional para um Lab mínimo, mas recomendado.

Endpoints mínimos:

```txt
GET  /status
GET  /daily-state
GET  /ghosts
GET  /evidence
GET  /receipts
GET  /canon
GET  /runtimes
POST /acts
POST /ghosts
POST /evidence
POST /receipts/prepare
POST /projectors/run
POST /clock/tick
POST /dispatch/prepare
POST /workorders/prepare
```

Regra:

```txt
labd may emit acts to Supabase.
labd may run projectors.
labd may prepare dispatch.
labd may not silently execute protected consequence.
```

---

## 10. Projectors

Projectors transformam acts em mundos legíveis.

Projectors podem ser:

```txt
SQL views
SQL functions
server jobs
Edge Functions
Node workers
Rust workers
manual bootstrap jobs
```

Projectors não podem:

```txt
invent evidence
authorize execution
close receipts
mutate canon
rewrite act meaning
```

Projectors mínimos:

```txt
project_registry_entities
project_registry_runtimes
project_ghost_board
project_evidence_records
project_receipt_index
project_daily_lab_state
project_mobile_today
```

---

## 11. Ghosts

Ghost é ausência preservada.

Ghost registry é projeção a partir de acts.

Ato típico:

```json
{
  "who": "santo-andre-laboratory",
  "did": "open_ghost",
  "this": {
    "ghost_key": "labd-interface-unimplemented",
    "what_missing": "No labd status endpoint is connected.",
    "why_it_matters": "Frontend cannot observe live Lab state.",
    "blocks": "runtime-observed Daily Lab State",
    "next_act": "implement labd status endpoint"
  },
  "when": "2026-05-28T00:00:00Z",
  "confirmed_by": {
    "source": "operator_observation"
  },
  "if_ok": {
    "project": "lab_observability.ghosts"
  },
  "if_doubt": {
    "carry": true
  },
  "if_not": {
    "reject": "ghost_without_missing_condition"
  },
  "status": "open"
}
```

---

## 12. Evidence

Evidence é observação referenciável.

Ato típico:

```json
{
  "who": "hermes-runtime",
  "did": "report_execution_result",
  "this": {
    "workorder_id": "wo_123",
    "exit_code": 0,
    "stdout_ref": "artifact://...",
    "stderr_ref": "artifact://...",
    "diff_hash": "sha256:...",
    "secret_redacted": true
  },
  "when": "2026-05-28T00:00:00Z",
  "confirmed_by": {
    "runtime_id": "hermes-local"
  },
  "if_ok": {
    "project": "evidence.records"
  },
  "if_doubt": {
    "open_ghost": "evidence-inconclusive"
  },
  "if_not": {
    "reject": "unredacted_or_invalid_execution_report"
  },
  "status": "observed"
}
```

Evidence não é receipt.

---

## 13. Receipts

Receipt é closure estreito.

Receipt candidate só pode nascer se houver evidence refs.

Ato típico:

```json
{
  "who": "receipt-reviewer",
  "did": "prepare_receipt_candidate",
  "this": {
    "claim": "Command cargo test ran on LAB512 with exit_code 0 at this time.",
    "scope_closed": "single command execution",
    "scope_not_closed": [
      "production readiness",
      "future behavior",
      "all regressions absent"
    ],
    "evidence_refs": ["evidence://..."],
    "ghosts_remaining": []
  },
  "when": "2026-05-28T00:00:00Z",
  "confirmed_by": {
    "evidence_refs": ["evidence://..."]
  },
  "if_ok": {
    "project": "receipts.candidates"
  },
  "if_doubt": {
    "open_ghost": "receipt-scope-unclear"
  },
  "if_not": {
    "reject": "broad_claim_from_narrow_evidence"
  },
  "status": "candidate"
}
```

---

## 14. Clock

O Lab tem clock.

Clock não é autoridade.

Clock pode:

```txt
emit tick acts
run status projections
find stale ghosts
prepare Daily Lab State
prepare Daily Expedition
surface next safe act
```

Clock não pode:

```txt
execute protected action
close receipt
delete ghost
publish
mutate provider
```

Comando:

```bash
logline-lab clock tick
```

Ato típico:

```json
{
  "who": "lab-clock",
  "did": "tick",
  "this": {
    "lab_id": "santo-andre-laboratory",
    "tick_kind": "daily",
    "checks": [
      "open_ghosts",
      "receipt_candidates",
      "runtimes",
      "evidence",
      "hooks"
    ]
  },
  "when": "2026-05-28T09:00:00Z",
  "confirmed_by": {
    "runtime_id": "logline-lab-cli"
  },
  "if_ok": {
    "project": "audit.v_daily_lab_state"
  },
  "if_doubt": {
    "open_ghost": "clock-check-inconclusive"
  },
  "if_not": {
    "reject": "invalid_clock_tick"
  },
  "status": "observed"
}
```

---

## 15. Hooks

Hooks são método obrigatório.

Não são UI hooks.

Exemplo:

```yaml
hook_id: before_receipt_review.require_evidence_refs.v1
trigger: before_lane.receipt_review
mandatory: true

checks:
  - evidence_refs_present
  - claim_scope_present
  - ghosts_remaining_named

on_pass:
  did: admit_receipt_review

on_fail:
  did: open_ghost
  ghost_key: receipt-review-evidence-missing
```

Hook missing bloqueia receipt.

---

## 16. Dispatch

Dispatch packet descreve trabalho.

Não executa.

Comando:

```bash
logline-lab dispatch prepare --process lab.health.check.v0
```

Dispatch packet mínimo:

```yaml
dispatch_version: logline.dispatch.v0
packet_id:
process_id:
organ:
office:
packet_type:
authority_level:
objective:
input_sources: []
expected_evidence: []
rollback_or_rectify:
required_human_check:
hermes:
  workorder_allowed:
  suggested_target_lab:
  suggested_mode:
allowed_actions: []
forbidden_actions: []
ghosts: []
```

---

## 17. Hermes workorder boundary

Hermes recebe workorders.

Não recebe chat.

Workorder mínimo:

```yaml
workorder_version: hermes.workorder.v0
workorder_id:
source_dispatch_packet:
authority_decision_ref:
execution_window_ref:
mode: read_only | dry_run | apply
target:
  lab_id:
  runtime_id:
  working_directory:
allowed_actions: []
forbidden_actions: []
commands:
  - command_id:
    kind:
    argv: []
    timeout_seconds:
expected_outputs: []
evidence_required: []
secret_policy:
  secret_values_allowed_in_logs: false
  redact_before_store: true
receipt_profile:
projection_targets: []
```

No apply without authority.

No protected without window.

No secrets in logs.

---

## 18. Study benches

O kit precisa incluir benches.

### Dialogue Observatory

Estuda conversas como intervalos de formação de atos.

### Interval Workbench

Estuda start/finish boundaries, simulations, real runs, result acts.

### Runtime Observatory

Estuda engines e runtimes.

### Projector Lab

Estuda como atos viram mundos.

### Composition Lab

Estuda polaridade, folding e entanglement de acts.

### Contract Bench

Estuda contratos como act graphs.

### Simulation Bench

Estuda Monte Carlo e simulações como runs envelopados.

### Standards Adapter Bench

Estuda projeções para W3C PROV, OpenTelemetry, RO-Crate, FHIR, EPCIS.

### Ghost Review

Estuda ausência preservada.

### Receipt Bench

Estuda closure estreito.

### Promotion Control

Estuda como artifacts viram trusted operational consequence.

---

## 19. Daily Lab Expedition

O kit deve gerar Daily Lab Expedition.

Comando:

```bash
logline-lab report generate daily-expedition
```

Inclui:

```txt
events
claims
evidence status
ghosts
receipt candidates
promotion state
next acts
operator packets
```

Não é receipt.

É relatório operacional.

---

## 20. Primeiro install flow

```bash
pnpm dlx logline-lab init
```

ou:

```bash
git clone <logline-lab-kit>
cd logline-lab-kit
pnpm install
cp .env.example .env
logline-lab init --manifest manifests/santo-andre.manifest.example.yaml
logline-lab doctor
logline-lab status
```

Resultado esperado:

```txt
Supabase connected
ops.logline_acts exists
registry schema exists
audit views exist
ghost registry projection exists
initial lab registration act emitted
initial ghosts opened
Daily Lab State available from Supabase projection
```

---

## 21. Primeiro ato do Lab

O init deve emitir:

```json
{
  "who": "dan",
  "did": "instantiate_logline_lab",
  "this": {
    "lab_id": "santo-andre-laboratory",
    "kit": "logline-lab-kit",
    "profile": "logline-lab.practice.v0",
    "semantic_write_spine": "ops.logline_acts",
    "projection_surface": "supabase"
  },
  "when": "2026-05-28T00:00:00Z",
  "confirmed_by": {
    "operator": "dan",
    "tool": "logline-lab init"
  },
  "if_ok": {
    "project": [
      "registry.entities",
      "audit.v_mobile_today",
      "lab_observability.current_state"
    ]
  },
  "if_doubt": {
    "open_ghost": "lab-instantiation-incomplete"
  },
  "if_not": {
    "reject": "invalid_lab_instantiation"
  },
  "status": "declared"
}
```

---

## 22. Acceptance criteria v0

O Lab Kit v0 é aceitável quando:

```txt
1. logline-lab init roda.
2. Supabase migrations criam ops.logline_acts.
3. Nenhum semantic write vai para fora de ops.logline_acts.
4. Pelo menos um Lab instance é registrado por LogLine Act.
5. Pelo menos um ghost é aberto por LogLine Act.
6. audit.v_mobile_today ou equivalente lê projeção real de Supabase.
7. logline-lab status retorna estado de Supabase.
8. logline-lab ghost list retorna ghosts projetados.
9. logline-lab act emit insere um ato nine-slot.
10. logline-lab doctor detecta schemas/projections ausentes.
11. Receipts não fecham sem evidence refs.
12. Hermes workorders não existem sem dispatch/admission boundary.
13. Frontends são opcionais.
14. minilab.work pode consumir o kit, mas não é o kit.
```

---

## 23. Build order

### Phase 0 - Skeleton

```txt
repo structure
README
manifest schema
.env.example
CLI skeleton
Supabase migrations
```

### Phase 1 - Act spine

```txt
ops.logline_acts migration
act emit command
doctor command
status command
```

### Phase 2 - Projections

```txt
registry.entities
registry.runtimes
lab_observability.ghosts
audit.v_mobile_today
```

### Phase 3 - Ghosts and Evidence

```txt
ghost open/list
evidence add/list
projection views
```

### Phase 4 - Receipts

```txt
receipt prepare
receipt blocked states
receipt index projection
```

### Phase 5 - Clock and Reports

```txt
clock tick
daily state
daily expedition report
weekly report
```

### Phase 6 - Dispatch/Hermes boundary

```txt
dispatch prepare
workorder prepare
execution report ingest
```

### Phase 7 - Frontend adapters

```txt
minilab.work reads Supabase projections
minilab.work emits act candidates through server path
```

## 24. Non-goals v0

Não implementar ainda:

```txt
full Hermes apply mode
full passkey windows
multi-user public SaaS
arbitrary database adapters
complete RLS authz model
all standards adapters
full AI office swarm
browser-based execution
```

## 25. Final formulation

```txt
The LogLine Lab Kit installs a living LogLine laboratory.

It loads canon.
It creates the Supabase act spine.
It emits LogLine Acts.
It projects state.
It preserves ghosts.
It captures evidence.
It prepares receipts.
It runs a clock.
It defines hooks.
It prepares dispatch.
It bounds Hermes.
It generates reports.
It studies LogLine in motion.

The frontend is optional.
The spine is Supabase.
The semantic unit is the LogLine Act.
```

---

## 26. Signature

```txt
We Trust and Build with LogLine.
```

A correção final é esta:

```txt
Não estamos desenhando “o backend da UI”.
Estamos desenhando o Kit que a UI consome.

O Kit instala o Lab.
O Supabase guarda os atos.
A CLI/labd opera.
Os projectors tornam legível.
minilab.work é só uma superfície.
```

Próximo ato seguro: **transformar essa spec em árvore real de repo + migrations iniciais + `logline-lab init/doctor/status/act emit`.**
